     <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

          <body>
               <div n="1" type="sthāna">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 1-31]</head>

                    <div n="1" type="adhyāya">

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.0"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.1">athāto vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||1|| </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ||2||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.3"> atha khalu bhagavantam amaravaram ṛṣigaṇaparivṛtam
                              āśramasthaṃ kāśirājaṃ divodāsaṃ dhanvantarim aupadhenava<pc
                                   > </pc>vaitaraṇaurabhra<pc> </pc>pauṣkalāvata<pc
                                   > </pc>-karavīrya<pc> </pc>gopurarakṣita<pc
                                   > </pc>suśruta<pc> </pc>prabhṛtaya ūcuḥ ||3|| <note
                                   type="footnote"> karavīra</note>
                         </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4"> bhagavan śārīramānasāgantuvyādhibhir
                              vividhavedanābhighātopadrutān sanāthān apy anāthavad viceṣṭamānān
                              vikrośataś ca mānavān abhisamīkṣya manasi naḥ pīḍā bhavati </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4b"> teṣāṃ sukhaiṣiṇāṃ rogopaśamārtham ātmanaś ca
                              prāṇayātrārthaṃ prajāhitahetor āyurvedaṃ śrotum icchāma
                              ihopadiśyamānaṃ atrāyattam aihikam āmuṣmikaṃ ca śreyaḥ tad bhagavantam
                              upapannāḥ smaḥ śiṣyatveneti ||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.5"> tān uvāca bhagavān svāgataṃ vaḥ sarva evāmīmāṃsyā
                              adhyāpyāś ca bhavanto vatsāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.6"> iha khalv āyurvedaṃ nāmopāṅgam
                              atharvavedasyānutpādyaiva prajāḥ ślokaśatasahasram adhyāyasahasraṃ ca
                              kṛtavān svayambhūḥ tato 'lpāyuṣṭvam alpamedhastvaṃ cālokya narāṇāṃ
                              bhūyo 'ṣṭadhā praṇītavān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.7"> tad yathā śalyaṃ śālākyaṃ kāyacikitsā bhūtavidyā
                              kaumārabhṛtyaṃ agadatantraṃ rasāyanatantraṃ vājīkaraṇatantram iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1"> athāsya pratyaṅgalakṣaṇasamāsaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1a"> tatra śalyaṃ nāma
                              vividhatṛṇakāṣṭhapāṣāṇapāṃśulohaloṣṭāsthibālanakhapūyāsrāvaduṣṭavraṇāntargarbhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ
                              yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānavraṇaviniścayārthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.2"> śālākyaṃ nāmordhvajatrugatānāṃ
                              śravaṇanayanavadanaghrāṇādisaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.3"> kāyacikītsā nāma sarvāṅgasaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnāṃ
                              jvararaktapittaśoṣonmādāpasmārakuṣṭhamehātisārādīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.4"> bhūtavidyā nāma
                              devāsuragandharvayakṣarakṣaḥpitṛpiśācanāgagrahādyupasṛṣṭacetasāṃ
                              śāntikarmabaloharaṇādigrahopaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.5"> kaumārabhṛtyaṃ nāma
                              kumārabharaṇadhātrīkṣīradoṣasaṃśodhanārthaṃ
                              duṣṭastanyagrahasamutthānāṃ ca vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.6"> agadatantraṃ nāma
                              sarpakīṭalūtāmūśikādidaṣṭaviṣavyañjanārthaṃ
                              vividhaviṣasaṃyogopaśamanārthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.7"> rasāyanatantraṃ nāma vayaḥsthāpanam
                              āyurmedhābalakaraṃ rogāpaharaṇasamarthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.8"> vājīkaraṇatantraṃ nāmālpaduṣṭakṣīṇaviśuṣkaretasām
                              āpyāyanaprasādopacayajanananimittaṃ praharṣajananārthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.9"> evam ayam āyurvedo 'ṣṭāṅga upadiśyate atra kasmai kim
                              ucyatām iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.10"> ta ūcuḥ asmākaṃ sarveṣām eva śalyajñānaṃ mūlaṃ
                              kṛtvopadiśatu bhagavān iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.11"> sa uvācaivam astv iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.12"> ta ūcur bhūyo 'pi bhagavantam asmākam ekamatīnāṃ
                              matam abhisamīkṣya suśruto bhagavantaṃ prakṣyati asmai copadiśyamānaṃ
                              vayam apy upadhārayiṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.13"> sa hovācaivam astv iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.14-16"> vatsa suśruta iha khalv āyurvedaprayojanaṃ
                              vyādhyupasṛṣṭānāṃ vyādhiparimokṣaḥ svasthasya rakṣaṇaṃ ca || āyur
                              asmin vidyate 'nena vā+āyur vindatīty āyurvedaḥ || tasyāṅgavaram ādyaṃ
                              pratyakṣāgamānumānopamānair aviruddham ucyamānam upadharaya || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17a"> etad dhy aṅgaṃ prathamaṃ prāg
                              abhighātavraṇasaṃrohāt yajñaśiraḥsandhānāc ca | śrūyate hi yathā
                              rudreṇa yajñasya śiraś chinnam iti </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17b"> tato devā aśvināv abhigamyocuḥ bhagavantau naḥ
                              śreṣṭhatamau yuvāṃ bhaviṣyathaḥ bhavadbhyāṃ yajñasya śiraḥ
                              sandhātavyam iti | tāv ūcatur evam astv iti | atha tayor arthe devā
                              indraṃ yajñabhagena prāsādayan | tābhyāṃ yajñasya śiraḥ saṃhitam iti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.18"> aṣṭāsv api cāyurvedatantreṣv etad evādhikam
                              abhimataṃ āmāśu kriyākaraṇād yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānāt
                              sarvatantrasāmānyāc ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.19"> tad idaṃ śāśvataṃ puṇyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ
                              vṛttikaraṃ ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20"> brahmā provāca tataḥ prajāpatir adhijage tasmād
                              aśvinau aśvibhyām indraḥ indrād aḥaṃ mayā tv iha pradeyam arthibhyaḥ
                              prajāhitahetoḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.21"> bhavati cātra | ahaṃ hi dhanvantarir ādidevo
                              jarārujāmṛtyuharo 'marāṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               śalyāṅgam aṅgair aparair upetaṃ prāpto 'smi gāṃ bhūya ihopadeṣṭum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.22"> asmin śāstre pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa
                              ity ucyate | tasmin kriyā so 'dhiṣṭhānaṃ kasmāt lokasya dvaividhyāt
                              loko hi dvividhaḥ sthāvaro jaṅgamaś ca dvividhātmaka evāgneyaḥ saumyaś
                              ca tadbhūyastvāt pañcātmako vā tatra caturvidho bhūtagrāmaḥ
                              saṃsvedajarāyujāṇḍajodbhijjasaṃjñaḥ tatra puruṣaḥ pradhānaṃ
                              tasyopakaraṇam anyat tasmāt puruṣo 'dhiṣṭhānam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.23"> tad duḥkhasaṃyogā vyādhaya ucyante || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.24"> te caturvidhāḥ āgantavaḥ śārīrāḥ mānasāḥ svābhāvikāś
                              ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.1"> teṣām āgantavo 'bhighātanimittāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.2"> śārīrās tv annapānamūlā
                              vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.3"> mānasās tu
                              krodhaśokabhayaharṣaviṣāderṣyābhyasūyādainyamātsaryakāmalobhaprabhṛtaya
                              icchādveṣabhedair bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.4"> svābhāvikās tu kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprakṛtayaḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.26"> ta ete manaḥśarīrādhiṣṭhānāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.27"> teṣāṃ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanāhārācārāḥ samyak prayuktā
                              nigrahahetavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.28"> prāṇināṃ punar mūlam āhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca sa
                              ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyattaḥ rasāḥ punar dravyāśrayāḥ dravyāṇi punar oṣadhayaḥ
                              | tās tu dvividhāḥ sthāvarā jaṅgamāś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.29"> tāsāṃ sthāvarāś caturvidhāḥ vanaspatayo vṛkṣā
                              vīrudha oṣadhaya iti | tāsu apuṣpāḥ phalavanto vanaspatayaḥ
                              puṣpaphalavanto vṛkṣāḥ pratānavatyaḥ stambinyaś ca vīrudhaḥ
                              phalapākaniṣṭhā oṣadhaya iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.30"> jaṅgamāḥ khalv api caturvidhāḥ
                              jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhijjāḥ | tatra paśumanuṣyavyālādayo jarāyujāḥ
                              khagasarpasarīsṛpaprabhṛtayo 'ṇḍajāḥ kṛmi<pc> </pc>kīṭa<pc
                                   > </pc>pipīlikā<pc> </pc>prabhṛtayaḥ svedajāḥ
                              indragopamaṇḍūkaprabhṛtaya udbhijjāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.31"> tatra sthāvarebhyas
                              tvakpatrapuṣpaphalamūlakandaniryāsasvarasādayaḥ prayojanavantaḥ
                              jaṅgamebhyaś carmanakharomarudhirādayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.32"> pārthivāḥ
                              suvarṇarajatamaṇimuktāmanaḥśilāmṛtkapālādayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.33"> kālakṛtāḥ
                              pravātanivātātapacchāyājyotsnātamaḥśītoṣṇavarṣāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanādayaḥ
                              saṃvatsaraviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.34"> ta ete svabhāvata eva doṣāṇāṃ
                              sañcayaprakopapraśamapratīkārahetavaḥ prayojanavantaś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35"> bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ
                              <caesura/>
                               śārīrāṇāṃ vikārāṇām eṣa vargaś caturvidhaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prakope praśame caiva hetur uktaś cikitsakaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.36"> āgantavas tu ye rogās te dvidhā nipatanti hi |
                              <caesura/>
                               manasy anye śarīre 'nye teṣāṃ tu dvividhā kriyā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.37"> śarīrapatitānāṃ tu śārīravad upakramaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               mānasānāṃ tu śabdādir iṣṭo vargaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.38"> evam etat puruṣo vyādhir auṣadhaṃ kriyā kāla iti
                              catuṣṭayaṃ samāsena vyākhyātam | tatra puruṣagrahaṇāt
                              tatsaṃbhavadravyasamūho bhūtādir uktas tadaṅgapratyaṅgavikalpāś ca
                              tvaṅmāṃsāsthisirāsnāyuprabhṛtayaḥ vyādhigrahaṇād
                              vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ sarva eva vyādhayo
                              vyākhyātāḥ oṣadhagrahaṇād dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākānām ādeśaḥ
                              kriyāgrahaṇāc chedyādīni snehādīni ca karmāṇi vyākhyātāni kālagrahaṇāt
                              sarvakriyākālānām ādeśaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               bījaṃ cikitsitasyaitat samāsena prakīrtitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam asya vyākhyā bhaviṣyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.40"> tac ca saviṃśam adhyāyaśataṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu
                              sūtranidānaśārīracikitsitakalpeṣv arthavaśāt saṃvibhajya uttare tantre
                              śeṣān arthān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41x"> </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               svayambhuvā proktam idaṃ sanātanaṃ
                              <caesura/>
                               paṭhed dhi yaḥ kāśipatiprakāśitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               sa puṇyakarmā bhuvi pūjito nṛpair
                              <caesura/>
                               asukṣaye śakrasalokatāṃ vrajet || </l>




                         <p xml:id="SS.1.1">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vedotpattir nāma
                              prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

                         <head>[dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ|]</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.1"> athātaḥ śiṣyopanayanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.3"> brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyānām anyatamam anvaya<pc
                                   > </pc>vayaḥ<pc/>śīla<pc> </pc>śaurya<pc
                                   > </pc>śaucācāra<pc> </pc>vinaya<pc> </pc>śakti<pc
                                   > </pc>bala<pc> </pc>medhā<pc> </pc>dhṛti<pc
                                   > </pc>smṛti<pc> </pc>mati<pc> </pc>pratipattiyuktaṃ
                                   tanu<pc> </pc>jihvauṣṭha<pc> </pc>dantāgram ṛjuvaktrākṣināsaṃ
                              prasannacittavākceṣṭaṃ kleśasahaṃ ca bhiṣak śiṣyam upanayet ato
                              viparītaguṇaṃ nopanayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.4"> upanayanīyaṃ tu brāhmaṇaṃ praśasteṣu
                              tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu praśastāyāṃ diśi śucau same deśe
                              caturhastaṃ caturasraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya gomayena darbhaiḥ saṃstīrya
                              puṣpair lājabhaktai ratnaiś ca devatāḥ pūjayitvā viprān bhiṣajaś ca
                              tatrollikhyābhyukṣya ca dakṣiṇato brahmāṇaṃ sthāpayitvā'gnim
                              upasamādhāya khadirapalāśadevadārubilvānāṃ samidbhiś caturṇāṃ vā
                              kṣīravṛkṣāṇāṃ (? nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthamadhūkānāṃ )
                              dadhimadhughṛtāktābhir dārvīhaumikena vidhinā sruveṇājyāhutīr juhuyāt
                              sapraṇavābhir mahāvyahṛtibhiḥ tataḥ pratidaivatamṛṣīṃś ca svāhākāraṃ
                              kuryāt śiṣyam api kārayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.5"> brāhmaṇas trayāṇāṃ varṇānām upanayanaṃ kartum arhati
                              rājanyo dvayasya vaiśyo vaiśyasyaiveti śūdram api kulaguṇasaṃpannaṃ
                              mantravarjam anupanītam adhyāpayed ity eke || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.6"> tato 'gniṃ triḥ pariṇīyāgnisākṣikaṃ śiṣyaṃ brūyāt
                              kāmakrodhalobhamohamānāhaṇkārerṣyāpāruṣyapaiśunyānṛtālasyāyaśasyāni
                              hitvā nīcanakharomṇā śucinā kaṣāyavāsasā
                              satyavratabrahmacaryābhivādanatatpareṇā'vaśyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ
                              madanumatasthānagamanaśayanāsanabhojanādhyayanapareṇa bhūtvā
                              matpriyahiteṣu vartitavyaṃ ato 'nyathā te vartamānasyādharmo bhavati
                              aphalā ca vidyā na ca prākāśyaṃ prāpnoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.7"> ahaṃ vā tvayi samyagvartamāne yady anyathādarśī syām
                              enobhāg bhaveyam aphalavidyaś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.8">
                              dvijagurudaridramitrapravrajitopanatasādhvanāthābhyupagatānāṃ
                              cātmabāndhavānām iva svabhaiṣajaiḥ pratikartavyam evaṃ sādhu bhavati
                              vyādhaśākunikapatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca na pratikartavyaṃ evaṃ vidyā
                              prakāśate mitra<pc> </pc>yaśo<pc> </pc>dharmārtha<pc> </pc>kāmāṃś ca
                              prāpnoti || </l>



                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.9"> bhavataś cātra | kṛṣṇe 'ṣṭamī tannidhane 'hanī dve
                              <caesura/>
                               śukle tathā 'py evam ahar dvisandhyam |
                              <caesura/>
                               akālavidyutstanayitnughoṣe
                              <caesura/>
                               svatantrarāṣṭrakṣitipavyathāsu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.2.10"> śmaśānayānādyatanāhaveṣu
                              <caesura/>
                               mahotsavautpātikadarśaneṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               nādhyeyam anyeṣu ca yeṣu vaprā
                              <caesura/>
                               nādhīyate nāśucinā ca nityam || </l>

                         <p xml:id="SS1.2.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śiṣyopanayanīyo
                              nāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="3" type="adhyāya">


                         <head>tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.1"> athāto 'dhyayanasaṃpradānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.3"> prāgabhihitaṃ saviṃśam adhyāyaśataṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu
                              | tatra sūtrasthānamadhyāyāḥ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśat ṣoḍśa nidānāni daśa
                              śārīrāṇi catvāriṃśaccikitsitāni aṣṭau kalpāḥ taduttaraṃ ṣaṭsāṣṭiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.4"> vedotpattiḥ śiṣyanayas tathā'dhyayanadānikaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prabhāṣaṇāgraharaṇāvṛtucaryātha yāntrikaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.5"> śastrāvacāaraṇaṃ yogyā viśikhā kṣārakalpanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               agnikarmajalaukākhyāvadhyāyau raktavarṇanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.6"> doṣadhātumalādyānāṃ vijñānādhyāya eva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               karṇavyadhāmapakvaiṣāvālepo vraṇyupāsanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.7"> hitāhito vraṇapraśno vraṇāsrāvaś ca yaḥ pṛthak |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṛtyākṛtyavidhirvyādhisamuddeśīya eva ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.8"> viniścayaḥ śastravidhau pranaṣṭajñānikas tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               śalyoddhṛtirvraṇajñānaṃ dūtasvapnanidarśanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.9"> pañcendriyaṃ tathā chāyā svabhāvādvaikṛtaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               vāraṇo yuktasenīya āturakramabhūnikau || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.10"> miśrakākhyo dravyagaṇaḥ saṃśuddhau śamane ca yaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dravyādīnāṃ ca vijñānaṃ viśeṣo dravyago 'paraḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.11"> rasajñānaṃ vamanārthamadhyāyo recanāya ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               dravaddravyavidhistadvadannapānavidhis tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.12"> sūcanāt sūtraṇāccaiva savanāccārthasantateḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadadhyāyaṃ sūtrasthānaṃ pracakṣate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.13"> vātavyādhikamarśāṃsi sāśmariś ca bhagandaraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               kuṣṭhamehodarā mūḍho vidradhiḥ parisarpaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.14"> granthivṛddhikṣudraśūkabhaknāś ca mukharogikam |
                              <caesura/>
                               hetulakṣaṇanirdeśānnidānānīti ṣoḍaśa || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.15"> bhūtacintā rajaḥśuddhirgarbhāvakrāntireva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               vyākaraṇaṃ ca garbhasya śarīrasya ca yatsmṛtam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.16"> pratyekaṃ marmanirdeśaḥ sirāvarṇanam eva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               sirāvyadho dhamanīnāṃ garbhiṇyā vyākṛtis tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.17"> nirdiṣṭāni daśaitāni śārīrāṇi maharṣiṇā |
                              <caesura/>
                               vijñānārthaṃ śarīrasya bhiṣajāṃ yoginām api || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.18"> dvivraṇīyo vraṇaḥ sadyo bhagnānāṃ vātarogikam |
                              <caesura/>
                               mahāvātikamarśāṃsi sāśmariś ca bhagandaraḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.19"> kuṣṭhānāṃ mahatāṃ cāpi maihikaṃ paiḍakaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               makhumehacikitsā ca tathā codariṇām api || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.20"> mūḍhagarbhacikitsā ca vidradhīnāṃ visarpiṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               granthivṛddhyupadaṃśānāṃ tathā ca kṣudrarogikam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.21"> śūkadoṣacikitsā ca tathā ca mukharogiṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               śophasyānāgatānāṃ ca niṣedho miśrakaṃ tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.22"> vājīkaraṃ ca yat kṣīṇe sarvābādhaśamo 'pi ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               medhāyuṣkaraṇaṃ cāpi svabhāvavyādhivāraṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.23"> nivṛttasaṃtāpakaraṃ kīrtitaṃ ca rasāyanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               snehopayaugikaḥ svedo vamane ca virecane || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.24"> tayor vyāpaccikitsā ca netrabastivibhāgikaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               netrabastivipatsiddhis tathā cottarabastikaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.25"> nirūhakramasaṃjñaś ca tathaivāturasaṃjñakaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhūmanasyavidhiś cāntyaś catvāriṃśad iti smṛtāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.26"> prāyaścittaṃ praśamanaṃ cikitsā śāntikarma ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               paryāyāstasya nirdeśāccikitsāsthānamucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.27"> annasya rakṣā vijñānaṃ sthāvarasyetarasya ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               sarpadaṣṭaviṣajñānaṃ tasyaiva ca cikitsitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.28"> dundubhermūṣikāṇāṃ ca kīṭānāṃ kalpa eva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               aṣṭau kalpāḥ samākhyātā viṣabheṣajakalpanāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.29"> adhyāyānāṃ śataṃ viṃśamevam etad udīritam |
                              <caesura/>
                               ataḥ paraṃ svanāmnaiva tantramuttaramucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.30"> adhikṛtya kṛtaṃ yasmāttantram etad upadravān |
                              <caesura/>
                               opadravika ity eṣa tasyāgryatvān nirucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.31"> sandhau vartmani śukle ca kṛṣṇe sarvatra dṛṣṭiṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃvijñānārthamadhyāyā gadānāṃ tu prati prati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.32"> cikitsāpravibhāgīyo vātābhiṣyandavāraṇaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               paittasya ślaiṣmikasyāpi raudhirasya tathaiva ca | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.33"> lekhyabhedyaniṣedhau ca chedyānāṃ vartmadṛṣṭiṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               kriyākalpo 'bhighātaś ca karṇotthāstaccikitsitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.34"> ghrāṇotthānāṃ ca vijñānaṃ tadgadapratiṣedhanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               pratiśyāyaniṣedhaś ca śirogadavivecanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.35"> cikitsā tadgadānāṃ ca śālākyaṃ tantramucyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               navagrahākṛtijñānaṃ skandasya ca niṣedhanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.36"> apasmāraśakunyoś ca revatyāś ca punaḥ pṛthak |
                              <caesura/>
                               pūtanāyās tathā'ndhāyā maṇḍikā śītapūtanā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.37"> naigameśacikitsā ca grahotpattiḥ sayonijā |
                              <caesura/>
                               kaumāratantram ity etac chārīreṣu ca kīrtitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.38"> jvarātisāraśoṣāṇāṃ gulmahṛdrogiṇām api |
                              <caesura/>
                               pāṇḍūnāṃ raktapittasya mūrcchāyāḥ pānajāś ca ye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.39"> tṛṣṇāyāś chardihikkānāṃ niṣedhaḥ śvāsakāsayoḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               svarabhedacikitsā ca kṛmyudāvartinoḥ prthak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.40"> visūcikārocakayor mūtrāghātavikṛcchrayoḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               iti kāyacikitsāyāḥ śeṣam atra prakīrtitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.41"> amānuṣaniṣedhaś ca tathā+āpasmāriko 'paraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               unmādapratiṣedhaś ca bhūtavidyā nirucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.42"> rasabhedāḥ svasthavṛttiryuktayastāntrikāś ca yāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               doṣabhedā iti jñeyā adhyāyāstantrabhūṣaṇāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.43"> śreṣṭhatvād uttaraṃ hy etat tantram āhur maharṣayaḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               bahvarthasaṃgrahāc chreṣṭham uttaraṃ cāpi paścimam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.44"> śālākyatantraṃ kaumāraṃ cikitsā kāyikī ca yā |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhūtavidyeti catvāri tantre tūttarasaṃjñite || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.45"> vājīkaraṃ cakitsāsu rasāyanavidhis tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               viṣatantraṃ punaḥ kalpāḥ śalyajñānaṃ samantataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.46"> ity aṣṭāṅgam idaṃ tantram ādidevaprakāśitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vidhinā'dhītya yuñjānā bhavanti prāṇadā bhuvi || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.47"> etad dhy avaśyam adhyeyaṃ adhītya ca karmāpy avaśyam
                              upāsitavyaṃ ubhayajño hi bhiṣak rājārho bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.48"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               yas tu kevalaśāstrajñaḥ karmasva pariniṣṭhitaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sa muhyaty āturaṃ prāpya prāpya bhīrur ivāhavam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.49"> yas tu karmasu niṣṇāto dhārṣṭyāc chāstrabahiṣkṛtaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sa satsu pūjāṃ nāpnoti vadhaṃ cārhati rājataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.50"> ubhāv etāv anipuṇāv asamarthau svakarmaṇi |
                              <caesura/>
                               ardhavedadharāv etāv ekapakṣāv iva dvijau || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.51"> oṣadhyo 'mṛtakalpās tu śastrāśaniviṣopamāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhavanty ajñair upahṛtās tasmād etān vivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.52"> snehādiṣv anabhijñā ye chedyādiṣu ca karmasu |
                              <caesura/>
                               te nihanti janaṃ lobhāt kuvaidyā nṛpadoṣataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.53"> yas tūbhayajño matimān sa samartho 'rthasādhane |
                              <caesura/>
                               āhave karma nirvoḍhuṃ dvicakraḥ syandano yathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.54"> atha vatsa tad etad adhyeyaṃ tathā tathopadhāraya
                              mayā procyamānaṃ atha śucaye
                              kṛtottarāsaṅgāyāvyākulayopasthitāyādhyayanakāle śiṣyāya yathāśakti
                              gurur upadiśet padaṃ pādaṃ ślokaṃ vā te ca padapādaślokābhūyaḥ
                              krameṇānusaṃdheyāḥ evam ekaikaśo ghaṭayed ātmanā cānupaṭhet adrutam
                              avilambitam aviśaṇkitam ananunāsikaṃ vyaktākṣram apīḍitavarṇam
                              akṣibhruvauṣṭhahastair anabhinītaṃ susaṃskṛtaṃ nātyuccair nātinīcaiś
                              ca svaraiḥ paṭhet | na cāntareṇa kaścid vrajet tayor adhīyānayoḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.55"> bhavataś cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               śucir guruparo dakṣas tandrānidrāvivarjitaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               paṭhann etena vidhinā śiṣyaḥ śāstrāntam āpnuyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.3.56"> vāksauṣṭhave 'rthavijñāne prāgalbhye karmanaipuṇe |
                              <caesura/>
                               tadabhyāse ca siddhau ca yatetādhyayanāntagaḥ || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāhaṃ sūtrasthāne 'dhyayanasaṃpradānīyo
                              nāma tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                    </div>

                    <div n="4" type="adhyāya">

                         <head>caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.1"> athātaḥ prabhāṣaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.2"> yāthovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.3"> adhigatam apy adhyayanam aprabhāṣitam arthataḥ
                              kharasya candanabhāra iva kevalaṃ pariśramakaraṃ bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.4"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               yathā kharaś candanabhāravāhī bhārasya vettā na tu candanasya |
                              <caesura/>
                               evaṃ hi śāstrāṇi baḥūny adhītya cārtheṣu mūḍhāḥ kharavad vahanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.5"> tasmāt saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam anupadapādaślokam
                              anuvarṇayitavyam anuśrotavyaṃ ca kasmāt sūkṣmā hi
                              dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākadoṣadhātumalāśayamarmasirāsnāyusandhyasthigarbhasaṃbhavadravyasamūhavibhāgās
                              tathā pranaṣṭaśalyoddharaṇavraṇaviniścayabhagnavikalpāḥ sādhyayāpy
                              apratyākhyeyatā ca vikārāṇām evam ādayaś cānye sahasraśo viśeṣā ye
                              vicintyamānā vimalavipulabuddher api buddhim ākulīkuryuḥ kiṃ punar
                              alpabuddheḥ tasmād avaśyam anupadapādaślokam anuvarṇayitavyam
                              anuśrotavyaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.6"> anyaśāstropapannānāṃ cārthānām ihopanītānām
                              arthavaśāt teṣāṃ tad vidyebhya eva vyākhyānam anuśrotavyaṃ kasmāt na
                              hy ekasmin śāstre śakyaḥ sarvaśāstrāṇām avarodhaḥ kartum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.7"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               ekaṃ śāstram adhīyāno na vidyāc chāstraniścayam |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmād bahuśrutaḥ śāstraṃ vijānīyāc cikitsakaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.8"> śāstraṃ gurumukhodgīrṇam ādāyopāsya cāsakṛt |
                              <caesura/>
                               yaḥ karma kurute vaiyaḥ sa vaidyo 'nye tu taskarāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.4.9"> aupadhenavam aurabhraṃ sauśrutaṃ pauṣkalāvatam |
                              <caesura/>
                               śeṣāṇāṃ śalyatantrāṇāṃ mūlāny etāni nirdiśet || </l>

                         <p ana="1.4.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne prabhāṣanīyo nāma
                              caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                    </div>

                    <div n="5" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.1"> athāto 'gropaharaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.3"> trividhaṃ karma pūrvakarma pradhānakarma
                              paścātkarmeti tadvyādhīṃ prati pratyupadekṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.4"> asmin śāstre śāstrakarmaprākhānyācchastrakarmaiva
                              tāvat pūrvam upadekṣyāmastatsambhārāṃś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.5"> tac ca śastrakarmā'ṣṭavidhaṃ tad yathā chedyaṃ
                              bhedyaṃ lekhyaṃ vedhyaṃ eṣyaṃ āhāryaṃ visrāvyaṃ sīvyam iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.6"> ato 'nyataṃ karma cikīrśatā vaidyena
                              pūrvamevopakalpayitavyāni
                              yantraśastrakṣārāgniśalākāśṛṅgajalaukālābūjāmbavauṣṭhapicuprotasūtrapatrapaṭṭamadhughṛtavasāpayastailatarpaṇakaṣāyālepanakalkavyajanaśītoṣṇodakakaṭāhādīni
                              parikarmiṇaś ca snigdhāḥ sthirā balavantaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.7"> tataḥ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu
                              dadhyakṣatānnapānaratnair agniṃ viprān miṣajaś cārcayitvā
                              kṛtabalimaṅgalasvastivācanaṃ laghubhuktavantaṃ prāṅnukhamāturam
                              upaveśya yantrayitvā pratyṅnukho vaidyo
                              marmasirāsnāyusandhyasthidhamanīḥ pariharan anulomaṃ śastraṃ
                              nidadhyādāpūyadarśanāt sakṛdevāpaharecchastramāśu ca mahatsv api ca
                              pākeṣu dvyaṅgulāntaraṃ tryaṅgulāntaraṃ vā śastrapadam uktam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.8"> tatrāyato viṣālaḥ samaḥ suvibhakto nirāśraya iti
                              vraṇaguṇāḥ </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.9"> bhavatś cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               āyataś ca viśālaś ca suvibhakto nirāśrayaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prāptakālakṛtaś cāpi vraṇaḥ karmaṇi śasyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.10"> śauryam āśukriyā śastrataikṣṇyam asvedavepathu |
                              <caesura/>
                               asaṃmohaś ca vaidyasya śastrakarmaṇi śasyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.11"> ekena vā vraṇenā'ṣudhyamāne nā'ntarā
                              buddhyā'vekṣyāparān vraṇān kuryāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.12"> bhavati cātra |

                               yato yato gatiṃ vidyādutsaṅgo yatra yatra ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               tatra tatra vraṇaṃ kuryād yathā doṣo na niṣṭhati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.13"> tatra
                              bhrūgaṇḍaśaṅkhalalāṭākṣipuṭauṣṭhadantaveṣṭakakṣākukṣivaṅkṣaṇeṣu tiyak
                              cheda uktaḥ || (?</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.14"> candramaṇḍalavacchedān pāṇipādeṣu kārayet |

                              cirādvraṇasaṃroho māṃsakandīprādurbhāvaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.16"> mūḍhagarbhodarārśo 'śmarībhagandaramukharogeṣv
                              abhuktavataḥ karma kurvīta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.17"> tataḥ śastram avacārya śītābhir adbhir āturam

                              kaṣāyeṇa protenodakam ādāya tilakalkamadhusarpiḥpragāḍhāmauṣadhayuktāṃ

                              dhūpair dhūpayet rakṣoghnaiś ca mantnrai rakṣāṃ kurvīta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.5.18"> tato guggulva<pc> </pc>guru<pc

                               tad vakṣyāmaḥ </l>

                    <div n="6" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>śaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.1"> athāta ṛtucaryam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.3"> kālo hi nāma bhagavān svayambhur anādimadhyanidhano
                              'tra rasavyāpatsampattī jīvitamaraṇe ca manuṣyāṇām āyatte | sa sūkṣmām
                              api kalāṃ na līyata iti kālaḥ saṃkalayati kālayati vā bhūtānīti kālaḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.4"> tasya saṃvatsarātmano bhagavān ādityo gativiśeṣeṇa
                              nimeṣakāṣṭhākalāmuhūrtāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanasaṃvatsarayugapravibhāgaṃ
                              karoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.5"> tatra laghvakṣaroccāraṇamātro 'kṣinimeṣaḥ
                              pañcadaśā'kṣinimeṣāḥ kāṣṭhā triṃśatkāṣṭhāḥ kalā viṃśatikalo muhūrtaḥ
                              kalādaśabhāgaś ca triṃśanmuhūrtam ahorātraṃ pañcadaśāhorātrāṇi pakṣaḥ
                              sa ca dvividhaḥ śuklaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca tau māsaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.6"> tatra māghādayo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ dvimāsikam
                              ṛtuṃ kṛtva ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti te śiśiravasantagrīṣmavarṣāśaraddhemantāḥ
                              teṣaṃ tapastapsyau śiśiraḥ madhumādhavau vasantaḥ śuciśukrau grīṣmaḥ
                              nabhonabhasyau varśāḥ iṣorjau śarat sahaḥsahasyau hemanta iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.7"> ta ete śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇāś candrād ity ayoḥ
                              kālavibhāgakaratvād ayane dve bhavato dakṣiṇam uttaraṃ ca | tayor
                              dakṣiṇaṃ varṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate somaḥ
                              amlalavaṇamadhurāś ca rasā balavanto bhavanti uttarottaraṃ ca
                              sarvaprāṇināṃ balam abhivardhate | uttaraṃ ca śiśiravasantagrīṣmāḥ
                              teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate 'rkaḥ tiktakaṣāyakaṭukāś ca rasā balavanto
                              bhavanti uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam apahīyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               śītāṃśuḥ kledayaty urvīṃ vivasvān śoṣayaty api |
                              <caesura/>
                               tāv ubhāv api saṃśritya vāyuḥ pālayati prajāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.9"> atha khalv ayane dve yugapat saṃvatsaro bhavati te tu
                              pañca yugam iti saṃjñāṃ labhante sa eṣa nimeṣādir yugaparyantaḥ kālaś
                              cakravat parivartamānaḥ kālacakram ucyata ity eke || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.10"> iha tu varṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmaprāvṛṣaḥ
                              ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti doṣopacayaprakopopaśamanimittaṃ te tu
                              bhādrapadādyena dvimāsikena vyākhyātāḥ tad yathā bhādrapadāśvayujau
                              varṣāḥ kārtikamārgaśīrṣau śarat pauṣamāghau hemantaḥ phālgunacaitrau
                              vasantaḥ vaiśākhajyeṣṭhau grīṣmaḥ āṣāḍhaśrāvaṇau prāvṛḍ iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.11"> tatra varṣāsv oṣadhayas taruṇyo 'lpavīryā āpaś
                              cāprasannāḥ kṣitimalaprāyāḥ tā upayujyamānā nabhasi meghāvatate
                              jalapraklinnāyāṃ bhūmau klinnadehānāṃ prāṇināṃ śīta<pc
                                   > </pc>vāta<pc> </pc>viṣṭambhitāgnīnāṃ vidahyante vidāhāt
                              pittasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayaḥ śaradi praviralameghe viyaty
                              upaśuṣyati paṅke 'rka<pc> </pc>kiraṇa<pc> </pc>pravilāyitaḥ paittikān
                              vyādhīn janayati | tā evauṣadhayaḥ kālapariṇāmāt pariṇatavīryā
                              balavatyo hemante bhavanty āpaś ca prasannāḥ snigdhā atyarthaṃ gurvyaś
                              ca tā upayujyamānā mandakiraṇatvād bhānoḥ satuṣārapa<pc
                                   > </pc>vanopa<pc> </pc>stambhita<pc> </pc>dehānāṃ dehinām
                              avidagdhāḥ snehāc chaityād gauravād upalepāc ca śleṣmasaṃcayam
                              āpādayanti sa saṃcayo vasante 'rka<pc> </pc>raśmi<pc> </pc>pravilāyita
                              īṣatstabdhadehānāṃ dehināṃ ślaiṣmikān vyādhīn janayati | tā
                              evauṣadhayo nidāghe niḥsārā rūkṣā atimātraṃ laghvyo bhavanty āpaś ca
                              tā upayujyamānāḥ sūryapratāpopaśoṣitadehānāṃ dehināṃ raukṣyāl
                              laghutvād vaiśadyāc ca vāyoḥ saṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayaḥ prāvṛṣi
                              cātyarthaṃ jalopaklinnāyāṃ bhūmau klinnadehānāṃ prāṇināṃ
                              śītavātavarṣerito vātikān vyādhīn janayati | evam eṣa doṣāṇāṃ
                              saṃcayaprakopahetur uktaḥ ||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.13"> tatra varśāhemantagrīṣmeṣu saṃcitānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ
                              śaradvasantaprāvṛṭsu ca prakupitānāṃ nirharaṇaṃ kartavyam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.14"> tatra paittikānāṃ vyādhīnām upaśamo hemante
                              ślaiṣmikāṇāṃ nidāghe vātikānāṃ śaradi svabhāvata eva ta ete
                              saṃcayaprakopopaśamā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.15"> tatra pūrvāhṇe vasantasya liṅgaṃ madhyāhne grīṣmasya
                              aparāhṇe prāvṛṣaḥ pradoṣe vārṣikāṃ śāradam ardharātre pratyuṣasi
                              haimantam upalakṣayet evam ahorātram api varṣam iva
                              śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇaṃ doṣopacayaprakopopaśamair jānīyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.16"> tatra avyāpanneṣv ṛtuṣv avyāpannā oṣadhayo bhavanty
                              āpaś ca tā upayujyamānāḥ prāṇāyurbalavīryaujaskaryo bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.17"> teṣāṃ punar vyāpado 'dṛṣṭakāritāḥ ṣītoṣṇavātavarṣāṇi
                              khalu viparītāny oṣadhīr vyāpādayanty apaś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.18"> tāsām upayogād vividharogaprādurbhāvo marako vā
                              bhaved iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.19"> tatra avyāpannānām oṣadhīnām apāṃ copayogaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.20"> kadācid avyāpanneṣv apy ṛtuṣu
                              kṛtyābhiśāparakṣaḥkrodhādharmair upadhvasyante janapadāḥ
                              viṣauṣadhipuṣpagandhena vāyunopanītenākramyate yo deśas tatra
                              doṣaprakṛtyaviśeṣeṇa kāsaśvāsavamathupratiśyāyaśirorugjvarair
                              upatapyante grahanakṣatracaritair vā
                              gṛhadāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbhāvair
                              vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.21"> tatra sthāna<pc> </pc>parityāga<pc
                                   > </pc>śāntikarma<pc> </pc>prāyaścitta<pc> </pc>maṅgala<pc

                                   > </pc>devatā<pc> </pc>brāhmaṇa<pc> </pc>guru<pc> </pc>parair
                              bhavitavyaṃ evaṃ sādhu bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.22"> ata ūrdhvam avyāpannānām ṛtūnāṃ lakṣaṇāny
                              upadekṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.23"> vāyur vāty uttaraḥ śīto rajodhūmākulā diśaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               channas tuṣāraiḥ saviyā himānaddhā jalāśayāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.24"> darpitā dhvāṅkṣakhaṅgāhvamahiṣorabhrakuñjarāḥ |
                              <caesura/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.25"> śiśire śītam adhikaṃ vātavṛṣṭyākulā diśaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               śeṣaṃ hemantavat sarvaṃ vijñeyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ budhaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.26"> siddhavidyādharavadhūcaraṇālaktakāṅkite |
                              <caesura/>
                               malaye candanalatāpariṣvaṅgādhivāsite || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.6.27"> vāti kāmijanānandajanano 'naṅgadīpanaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dampatyor mānabhiduro vasante dakṣiṇo 'nilaḥ || </l>

                              <caesura/>
