                    <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.1"> athātaḥ śoṇitavarṇanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.3"> tatra pāñcabhautikasya caturvidhasya ṣaḍrasasya
                              dvividhavīryasyāṣṭavidhāvīryasya vā'nekaguṇasyopayuktasyāhārasya
                              samyakpariṇatasya yas tejobhūtaḥ sāraḥ paramasūkṣmaḥ sa rasa ity
                              ucyate tasya ca hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ sa hṛdayāc caturviṃśati dhamanīr
                              anupraviśyor dhvagā daśa daśa cādhogāminyaś catasraś ca tiryaggāḥ
                              kṛtsnaṃ śarīram aharahas tarpayati vardhayati dhārayati yāpayati
                              cādṛṣṭahetukena karmaṇā | tasya śarīram anusarato 'numānād gatir
                              upalakṣayitavyā kṣayavṛddhivaikṛtaiḥ | tasmin
                              sarvaśarīrāvayavadoṣadhātumalāśayānusāriṇi rase jijñāsā kim ayaṃ
                              saumyas taijasa iti | atrocyate sa khalu dravānusārī
                              snehanajīvanatarpaṇadhāraṇādibhir viśeṣaiḥ saumya ity avagamyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.4"> sa khalv āpyo raso yakṛtplīhānau prāpya rāgam upaiti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.5"> bhavataś cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               rañjitās tejasā tv āpaḥ śarīrasthena dehinām |
                              <caesura/>
                               avyāpannāḥ prasannena raktam ity abhidhīyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.6"> rasād eva striyā raktaṃ rajaḥsaṃjñaṃ pravartate |
                              tad varṣād dvyādaśād ūrdhvaṃ yāti pañcāśataḥ kṣayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.7"> ārtavaṃ śoṇitaṃ tv āgneyaṃ agnīṣomīyatvād garbhasya
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.8"> pāñcabhautikaṃ tv apare jīvaraktam āhur ācāryāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.9"> vesratā dravatā rāgaḥ spandanaṃ laghutā tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhūmyādīnāṃ guṇā hyete dṛśyante cātra śoṇite || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.10"> rasād raktaṃ tato māṃsaṃ māṃsān medaḥ prajāyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               medaso 'sthi tato majjā majjñaḥ śukraṃ tu jāyate || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.11"> tatraiṣāṃ (? sarva ) dhātūnām annapānarasaḥ
                              prīṇayitā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.12"> rasajaṃ puruṣaṃ vidyād rasaṃ rakṣet prayatnaḥ |
                              annāt pānāc ca matimān ācārāc cāpy atandritaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.13"> tatra rasa gatau dhātuḥ aharahar gacchatīty ato
                              rasaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.14"> sa khalu trīṇi trīṇi kalāsahasrāṇi pañcadaśa ca
                              kalā ekaikasmin dhātāv avatiṣṭhate evaṃ māsena rasaḥ śukrībhavati
                              strīṇāṃ cārtavam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.15"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               aṣṭādaśasahasrāṇi saṅkhyā hy asmin samuccaye |
                              <caesura/>
                               kalānāṃ navatiḥ proktā svatantraparatantrayoḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.16"> sa śabdārcir<pc> </pc>jala<pc> </pc>santānavad aṇunā viśeṣeṇānudhāvaty
                              evaṃ śarīraṃ kevalam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.17"> vājīkaraṇyas tv oṣadhayaḥ svabalaguṇotkarṣād
                              virecanavad upayuktāḥ śukraṃ virecayanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.18"> yathā hi puṣpamukulastho gandho na śakyam ihāstīti
                              vaktum atho naivā(ā.naiva cā)stīti athavā'(? ca)sti satāṃ bhāvānām
                              abhivyaktir iti kṛ(ā.jñā)tvā kevalaṃ saukṣmyān nābhivyajyate sa eva
                              puṣpe vivṛtapatrakeśare kālāntareṇābhivyaktiṃ gacchati evaṃ bālānām
                              api vayaḥpariṇāmāc chukraprādurbhāvo bhavati romarājyādayaś ca viśeṣā
                              nārīṇām | (? rajasi copacīyamāne śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
                              stanagarbhāśayayonyabhivṛddhir bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.19"> sa evānnaraso vṛddhānāṃ (? jarā)paripakvaśarīratvād
                              aprīṇano bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.20"> ta ete śrīradhāraṇād dhātava ity ucyante || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.21"> teṣāṃ kṣayavṛddhī śoṇitanimitte tasmāt tad
                              adhikṛtya vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra phanilamaruṇaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ parūṣaṃ tanu
                              śīghragamaskandi ca vātena duṣṭaṃ nīlaṃ pītaṃ haritaṃ śyāvaṃ
                              visramaniṣṭaṃ pipīlikāmakṣikāṇāmaskandi ca pittaduṣṭaṃ
                              gairikodakapratīkāśaṃ snigdhaṃ śītalaṃ bahalaṃ picchilaṃ cirasrāvi
                              māṃsapeśīprabhaṃ ca śleṣmaduṣṭaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ kāñjikābhaṃ
                              viśeṣato durgandhi ca sannipātaduṣṭaṃ (? pittavadraktenātikṛṣṇaṃ ca)
                              dvidoṣaliṅgaṃ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ | (? jīvaśoṇitamanyatra vakṣyāmaḥ )// </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.22"> indragopakapratīkāśamasaṃhatamavivarṇaṃ ca
                              prakṛtisthaṃ jānīyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.23"> visrāvyāṇyanyatra vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.24"> athāvisrāvyāḥ sarvāṅgaśophaḥ kṣīṇasya
                              cāmlabhojananimittaḥ pāṇdurogyarśasodariśoṣigarbhiṇīnāṃ ca śvayathavaḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.25"> tatra śastravisrāvaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ pracchānaṃ
                              sirāvyadhanaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.26"> tatra ṛjvasaṃkīrṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ samam anavagāḍham
                              anuttānam āśu ca śastraṃ pātayen marmasirāsnāyusandhīnāṃ cānupaghāti
                              || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.26a"/>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.26b"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.27"> tatra durdine durviddhe śītavātayor asvinne
                              bhuktamātre skandatvāc choṇitaṃ na sravaty alpaṃ vā sravati || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.28"> madamūrcchāśramārtānāṃ vāta<pc> </pc>viṇ<pc
                              > </pc>mūtrasaṃginām |
                              <caesura/>
                               nidrābhibhūtabhītānāṃ nṛṇāṃ nāsṛk pravartate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.29"> tad duṣṭaṃ śoṇitamanirhriyamāṇaṃ
                              kaṇḍūśopharāgadāhapākavedanā janayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.30"> atyuṣṇe 'tisvinne 'tividdhe 'jñair
                              vasrāvitamatipravartate tad atipravṛttaṃ śiro
                              'bhitāpamāndhyamadhimanthatimiraprādurbhāvaṃ dhātukṣayamākṣepakaṃ
                              pakṣāghātamekāṅgavikāraṃ tṛṣṇādāhau hikkāṃ kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ pāṇḍurogaṃ
                              maraṇaṃ cāpādayati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.30a"> bhavanti cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.31"> tasmānna śite nātyuṣṇe nāsvinne nātitāpite |
                              <caesura/>
                               yavāgūṃ pratipītasya śoṇitaṃ mokṣayed bhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.32"> samyag gatvā yadā raktaṃ svayam evāvatiṣṭhate |
                              <caesura/>
                               śuddhaṃ tadā vijānīyāt samyagvisrāvitaṃ ca tat || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.33"> lāghavaṃ vedanāśāntirvyādhervegaparikṣayaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               samyagvisrāvite liṅgaṃ prasādo manasas tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.34"> tvagdoṣā granthayaḥ śophā rogāḥ śoṇitajāś ca ye |
                              <caesura/>
                               raktamokṣaṇaśīlānāṃ na bhavanti kadācana || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.35"> atha khalvapravartamāne rakte
                              elāśītaśivakuṣṭhatagarapāṭhābhadradāruviḍaṅgacitrakatrikaṭukāgāradhūmaharidrārkāṅkuranaktamālaphalair
                              yathālābhaṃ tribhiś caturbhiḥ samastair vā cūrṇīkṛtair
                              lavanātailapragāḍhair vraṇamukham avagharṣayed evaṃ samyak pravartate
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.36"> athātipravṛtte
                              rodhramadhukapriyaṅgupattaṅgagairikasarjarasarasāñjanaśālmalīpuṣpaśaṅkhaśuktimāṣayavagodhūmacūrṇaiḥ
                              śanaiḥ śanair vraṇamukham avacūrṇyāṅgulyagreṇāvapīḍayet
                              sālasarjārjūnārimedameṣaśṛnṅgadhavadhanvantvagbhir vā cūrṇitābhiḥ
                              kṣaumeṇa vā dhmāpitena samudraphenalākṣācūrṇair vā yathoktair
                              vraṇabandhanadravyair gāḍhaṃ badhnīyāt śītāccchādanabhojanāgāraiḥ
                              śītaiḥ pariṣekapradehaiś copācaret kṣārenāgninā vā dahedyathoktaṃ
                              vyadhanādanantaraṃ vā tāmevātipravṛttāṃ sirāṃ vidhyet kākolyādikvāthaṃ
                              vā śarkarāmadhumadhuraṃ pāyayet eṇahariṇorabhraśaśamahiṣavarāhāṇāṃ vā
                              rudhiraṃ kṣirayūṣarasaiḥ susnigdhaiś cāśnīyāt upadravāṃś ca yathāsvam
                              upacaret || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.37"> dhātukṣayāt srute rakte mandaḥ saṃjāyate 'nalaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pavanaś ca paraṃ lopaṃ yāti tasmāt prayatnaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.38"> taṃ nātiśītair laghubhiḥ snigdhaiḥ śoṇitavardhanaiḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               īṣadamlair anamlair vā bhojanaiḥ samupācaret || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.39"> caturvidhaṃ yad etad dhi rudhirasya nivāraṇam |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃdhānaṃ skandanaṃ caiva pācanaṃ dahanaṃ tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.40"> vraṇaṃ kaṣāyaḥ saṃdhatte raktaṃ skandayate himam |
                              <caesura/>
                               tathā saṃpācayed bhasma dāhaḥ saṃkocayet sirāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.41"> askandamāne rudhire saṃdhānāni prayojayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃdhāne bhraśyamāne tu pācanaiḥ samupācaret | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.42"> kalpair etais tribhir vaidyaḥ prayateta yathāvidhi
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               asiddhimatsu caiteṣu dāhaḥ parama iṣyate | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.43"> śeṣadoṣe yato rakte na vyādhirativartate |
                              <caesura/>
                               sāvaśeṣe tataḥ stheyaṃ na tu kuryād atikramam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.44"> dehasya rudhiraṃ mūlaṃ rudhireṇaiva dhāryate |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmād yatnena saṃrakṣyaṃ raktaṃ jīva iti sthitiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.14.45"> srutaraktasya sekādyaiḥ śītaiḥ prakupite 'nile |
                              <caesura/>
                               śophaṃ satodaṃ loṣṇena sarpiṣā pariṣecayet ||</l>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śoṇitavarṇanīyo nāma
                              caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="15" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.1"> athāto doṣadhātumalakṣayavṛddhivijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ
                              vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.3"> doṣadhātumalamūlaṃ hi śarīraṃ tasmād eteṣāṃ
                              lakṣaṇamucyamānam upadhāraya || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.4.1"> tatra praspandanodvahanapūranāvivekadhāraṇalakṣaṇo
                              vāyuḥ pañcadhā pravibhaktaḥ śarīraṃ dhārayati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.4.2"> rāgapaktyojastejomedhoṣmakṛtpittaṃ pañcadhā
                              pravibhaktam agnikarmaṇānugrahaṃ karoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.4.3">
                              sandhisaṃśleṣaṇasnehanaropaṇapūraṇabalasthairyakṛcchleṣmā pañcadhā
                              pravibhakta udakakarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ karoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.5"> rasas tuṣṭiṃ prīṇanaṃ raktapuṣṭiṃ ca karoti raktaṃ
                              varṇaprasādaṃ māṃsapuṣṭiṃ jīvayati ca māṃsaṃ śarīrapuṣṭiṃ medasaś ca
                              medaḥ snehasvedau dṛḍhatvaṃ puṣṭim asthnāṃ ca asthīni dehadhāraṇaṃ
                              majjñaḥ puṣṭiṃ ca majjā prītiṃ snehaṃ balaṃ śukrapuṣṭiṃ pūraṇam
                              asthnāṃ ca karoti śukraṃ dhairyaṃ cyavanaṃ prītiṃ dehabalaṃ harṣaṃ
                              bījārthaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.6"> purīṣam upastambhaṃ vāyvagnidhāraṇaṃ ca
                              bastipūraṇavikledakṛn mūtraṃ svedaḥ kledatvaksaukumāryakṛt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.7"> raktalakṣaṇam ārtavaṃ garbhakṛc ca garbho
                              garbhalakṣaṇaṃ stanyaṃ stanayor āpīnatvajananaṃ jīvanaṃ ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.8"> tatra vidhivat parirakṣaṇaṃ kurvīta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.9"> ata ūrdhvam eṣāṃ kṣīṇalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra
                              vātakṣaye mandaceṣṭatā'lpāvāktvam apraharṣo mūḍhasaṃjñatā ca
                              pittakṣaye mandoṣmāgnitā niṣprabhatvaṃ(ā.tā) ca śleṣmakṣaye
                              rūkṣatā'ntardāha āmāśayetaraśleṣmāśayaśūnyatā sandhiśaithilyaṃ tṛṣṇā
                              daurbalyaṃ prajāgaraṇaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.10"> tatra svayonivardhanāny eva pratīkāraḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.11"> rasakṣaye hṛtpīḍā<pc> </pc>kampaśūnyātās tṛṣṇā ca
                              śoṇitakṣaye tvakpāruṣyam amlaśītaprārthanā sirāśaithilyaṃ ca
                              māṃsakṣaye sphiggaṇḍauṣṭhopasthoruvakṣaḥ<pc
                              > </pc>kakṣāpiṇḍikodaragrīvāśuṣkatā raukṣyatodau gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ
                              dhamanīśaithilyaṃ ca medaḥkṣaye plīhābhivṛddhiḥ sandhiśūnyatā raukṣyaṃ
                              meduramāṃsaprārthanā ca asthikṣaye 'sthiśūlaṃ dantanakhabhaṅgo
                              raukṣyaṃ ca majjakṣaye 'lpaśukratā parvabhedo 'sthinistodo
                              'sthiśūnyatā ca śukrakṣaye meḍhravṛṣaṇavedanā'śaktirmaithune cirād vā
                              prasekaḥ praseke cālparaktaśukradarśanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.12"> tatrāpi svayonivardhanadravyopayogaḥ pratīkāraḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.13"> purīṣakṣaye hṛdayapārśvapīḍā saśabdasya ca vāyor
                              ūrdhvagamanaṃ kukṣau saṃcaraṇaṃ ca mūtrakṣaye bastitodo 'lpamūtratā ca
                              atrāpi svayonivardhanadravyāṇi pratīkāraḥ | svedakṣaye
                              stabdharomakūpatā tvakśoṣaḥ sparśavaiguṇyaṃ svedanāśaś ca
                              tatrābhyaṅgaḥ svedopayogaś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.14"> ārtavakṣaye yathocitakālādarśanamalpatā vā
                              yonivedanā ca tatra saṃśodhanamāgneyānāṃ ca dravyāṇāṃ vidhivadupayogaḥ
                              | stanyakṣaye stnayor mlānatā stanyāsaṃbhavo 'lpatā vā tatra
                              śleṣmavardhanadravyopayogaḥ | garbhakṣaye
                              garbhāspandanamanunnatakukṣitā ca tatra prāptabastikālāyāḥ
                              kṣīrabastiprayogo medhyānnopayogaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.15"> ata ūrdhvam ativṛddhānāṃ doṣadhātumalānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ
                              vakṣyāmaḥ | vṛddhiḥ punar eṣāṃ svayonivardhanātyupasevanād bhavati |
                              tatra vātavṛddhau vākpāruṣyaṃ kārśyaṃ kārṣṇyaṃ gātrasphuraṇam
                              uṣṇakāmitā nidrānāśo 'lpabalatvaṃ gāḍhavarcastvaṃ ca pittavṛddhau
                              pītāvabhāsatā saṃtāpaḥ śītakāmitvam alpanidratā mūrcchā balahānir
                              indriyadaurbalyaṃ pītaviṇmūtranetratvaṃ ca śleṣmavṛddhau śauklyaṃ
                              śaityaṃ sthairyaṃ gauravam avasādas tandrā nidrā sandhyasthiviśleṣaś
                              ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.16"> raso 'tivṛddho hṛdayotkledaṃ prasekaṃ cāpādayati
                              raktaṃ raktāṅgākṣitāṃ sirāpūrṇatvaṃ ca māṃsaṃ
                              sphiggaṇḍauṣṭhopasthorubāhujaṅghāsu vṛddhiṃ gurugātratāṃ ca medaḥ
                              snigdhāṅgatāmudarapārśvavṛddhiṃ kāsaśvāsādīn daurgandhyaṃ ca
                              asthyadhyasthīnyadhidantāṃś ca majjā sarvāṅganetragauravaṃ ca śukraṃ
                              śukrāśmarīmatiprādurbhāvaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.17"> purīṣamāṭopaṃ kukṣau śūlaṃ ca mūtraṃ mūtravṛddhiṃ
                              muhurmuhuḥ pravṛttiṃ bastitodamādhmānaṃ ca svedastvaco daugandhyaṃ
                              kaṇḍūṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.18"> ārtavam aṅgamardam atipravṛttiṃ daurgandhyaṃ ca
                              stanyaṃ stanayor āpīnatvaṃ muhur muhuḥ pravṛttiṃ todaṃ ca garbho
                              jaṭharābhivṛddhiṃ svedaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.19"> teṣāṃ yathāsvaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ kṣapaṇaṃ ca kṣayād
                              aviruddhaiḥ kriyāviśeṣaiḥ prakurvīt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.20"> pūrvaḥ pūrvo 'tivṛddhatvād vardhayed dhi paraṃ
                              param |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasam ātipravṛddhānāṃ dhātūnāṃ hrāsanaṃ hitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.21"> balalakṣaṇaṃ balakṣayalakṣaṇaṃ cāta ūrdhvam
                              upadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra rasādīnāṃ śukrāntānāṃ dhātūnāṃ yat paraṃ tejas
                              tat khalv ojas tad eva balam ity ucyate svaśāstrasiddhāntāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.22"> tatra balena sthiropacitamāṃsatā
                              sarvaceṣṭāsvapratighātaḥ svaravarṇaprasādo bāhyānām ābhyantarāṇāṃ ca
                              karaṇānām ātmakāryapratipattir bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.23"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               ojaḥ somātmakaṃ snigdhaṃ śuklaṃ śītaṃ sthiraṃ saram |
                              <caesura/>
                               viviktaṃ mṛdu mṛtsnaṃ ca prāṇāyatanam utttamam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.24ab"> dehaḥ sāvayavas tena vyāpto bhavati dehinām |</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.24cd"> tadabhāvāc ca śīryante śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25abcd"> abhighātāt kṣayāt kopāc chokād dhyānāc chramāt
                              kṣudhaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ojaḥ saṃkṣīyate hy ebhyo dhātugrahaṇaniḥsṛtam |</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25ef"> tejaḥ samīritaṃ tasmād visraṃsayate dehinaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.26-27"> tasya visraṃso vyāpat kṣaya iti liṅgāni
                              vyāpannasya bhavanti sandhiviśleṣo gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ doṣacyavanaṃ
                              kriyā'(O.kriyā)sannirodhaś ca visraṃse stabdhagurugātratā vātaśopho
                              varṇabhedo glānis tandrā nidrā ca vyāpanne mūrcchā māṃsakṣayo mohaḥ
                              pralāpo maraṇam iti ca kṣaye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               trayo doṣā balasyoktā vyāpadvisraṃsanakṣayāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               viśleṣasādau gātrāṇāṃ doṣavisraṃsanaṃ śramaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               aprācuryaṃ kriyānāṃ ca balavisraṃsalakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.29"> gurutvaṃ stabdhatā'ṇgeṣu glānirvarṇasya bhedanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               tandrā nidrā vātaśopho balavyāpadi lakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.30"> mūrcchā māṃsakṣāyo mohaḥ pralāpo 'jñānam eva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               pūrvoktāni ca liṅgāni maraṇaṃ ca balakṣaye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.31"> tatra visraṃse vyāpanne ca kriyāviśeṣair
                              aviruddhair balamāpyāyayet itaraṃ tu mūḍhasaṃjñaṃ varjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.32"> doṣadhātumalakṣīṇo balakṣīṇi'pi vā naraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               svayonivardhanaṃ yattadannapānaṃ prakāṅkṣati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.33"> yadyadāhārajātaṃ tu kṣīṇaḥ prārthayate naraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasya tasya sa lābhe tu taṃ taṃ kṣayamapohati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.34"> yasya dhātukṣayād vāyuḥ saṃjñāṃ karma ca nāśayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               prakṣiṇaṃ ca balaṃ yasya nāsu śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.35"> rasanimittam eva sthaulyaṃ kārśyaṃ ca | tatra
                              śleṣmalāhārasevino 'dhyaśanaśīlasyāvyāyāmino divāsvapnaratasya cāma
                              evānnaraso madhurataraś ca śarīram anukrāmann atisnehān medo janayati
                              tad atisthaulyam āpādayati tam atisthūlaṃ
                              kṣudraśvāsapipāsākṣutsvapnasvedagātradaurgandhyakrathanagātrasādagadgadatvāni
                              kṣipram evāviśanti saukumāryān medasaḥ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaḥ
                              kaphamedo niruddhamārgartvāc cālpavyavāyo bhavati āvṛtamārgatvād eva
                              śeṣā dhātavo nāpyāyante 'tyarthamato 'lpaprāṇo bhavati
                              pramehapīḍakājvarabhagandaravidradhivātavikārāṇāmanyataṃ prāpya
                              pañcatvam upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty
                              āvṛtamārgatvāt srotasāṃ atas tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                              śilājatuguggulugomūtratriphalāloharajorasāñjanamadhuyavamudgakoradūṣakaśyāmākoddālakādīnāṃ
                              virūkṣaṇacchedanīyānāṃ dravyāṇaṃ vidhivad upayogo vyāyāmo
                              lekhanabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.36"> tatra punar vātalāhārasevino
                              'tivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanabhayaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇapipāsākṣutkaṣāyālpāśanaprabhṛtibhir
                              upaśoṣito rasadhātuḥ śarīram ananukrāman nalpatvān na prīṇāti tasmād
                              atikārśyaṃ bhavati so 'tikṛśaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavātavarṣabhārādāneṣv
                              asahiṣṇur vātarogaprāyo 'lpaprāṇaś ca kriyāsu bhavati
                              śvāsakāsaśoṣaplīhodarāgnisādagulmaraktapittānām anyatamam āsādya
                              maraṇam upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty alpaprāṇatvāt
                              atas tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                              payasyāśvagandhāvidārigandhāśatāvarībalātibalānāgabalānāṃ madhurāṇām
                              anyāsaṃ cauṣadhīnām upayogaḥ
                              kṣīradadhighṛtamāṃsaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmānāṃ ca
                              divāsvapnabrahmacaryāvyāyāmabṛhaṇabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.37"> yaḥ punar ubhayasādhāraṇāny āseveta tasyān narasaḥ
                              śarīram anukrāman samān dhātūn upacinoti samadhātutvān madhyaśarīro
                              bhavati sarvakriyāsu samarthaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavarṣātapasaho balavāṃś
                              ca sa satatam anupālayitavya iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.38"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               atyantagarhitāv etau sadā sthūlakṛśau narau |
                              <caesura/>
                               śreṣṭho madhyaśarīras tu kṛśaḥ sthūlāt tu pūjitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.39"> doṣaḥ prakupito dhātūn kṣapayaty ātmatejasā |
                              <caesura/>
                               iddhaḥ svatejasā vahnir ukhāgatam ivodakam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.40"> vailakṣaṇyāc charīrāṇām asthāyitvāt tathaiva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               doṣadhātumalānāṃ tu parimāṇaṃ na vidyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.41"> eṣāṃ samatvaṃ yac cāpi bhiṣagbhir avadhāryate |
                              <caesura/>
                               na tat svāsthyādṛte śakyaṃ vaktum anyena hetunā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.42"> doṣādīnāṃ tv asamatām anumānena lakṣayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               aprasannendriyaṃ vīkṣya puruṣaṃ kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43"> svasthasya rakṣaṇaṃ kuryād asvasthasya tu buddhimān
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣapayed bṛṃhayec cāpi doṣadhātumalān bhiṣak | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43ef"> tāvad yāvad arogaḥ syād etat sāmyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.15.44"> samadoṣaḥ samāgniś ca samadhātumalakriyaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prasannātmendriyamanāḥ svasthā ity abhidhīyate ||</l>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              doṣadhātumalakṣayavṛddhivijñānīyo nāma pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>

                    <div n="16" type="adhyāya">

                         <head>ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.1"> athātaḥ karṇavyadha<pc> </pc>bandha<pc> </pc>vidhim
                              adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanavatariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.3"> rakṣābhūṣaṇanimittaṃ bālasya karṇau vidhyete | tau
                              ṣaṣṭhe māsi saptame vā śuklapakṣe praśasteṣu
                              tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaṃ dhātryaṅke
                              kumāradharāṅke vā kumāram upaveśya bālakrīḍanakaiḥ
                              pralobhyābhisāntvayan bhiṣag vāmahastenākṛṣya karṇaṃ daivakṛte chidra
                              ādityakarāvabhāsite śanaiḥ śanair dakṣiṇahastena rju vidhyet
                              pratanukaṃ sūcyā bahalam ārayā pūrvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kumārasya vāmaṃ
                              kumāryāḥ tataḥ picuvartiṃ praveśayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.4"> śoṇita<pc> </pc>bahutvena vedanayā cānyadeśaviddham
                              iti jānīyāt nirupadravatayā taddeśaviddham iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.5"> tatrājñena yadṛcchayā viddhāsu sirāsu
                              kālikāmarmarikālohitikāsūpadravā bhavanti | tatra kālikāyāṃ jvaro
                              dāhaḥ śvayathur vedanā ca bhavati marmarikāyāṃ vedanā jvaro granthayaś
                              ca lohitikāyāṃ manyāstambhāpatānakaśirograhakarṇaśūlāni bhavanti |
                              teṣu yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.6"> kliṣṭajihmāpraśastasūcīvyadhād gāḍhataravartitvād
                              doṣasamudāyād apraśastavyadhād vā yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati
                              tatra vartim upahṛtyāśu madhukairaṇḍa<pc> </pc>mūla<pc
                                   > </pc>mañjiṣṭhā<pc> </pc>yava<pc> </pc>tila<pc> </pc>kalkair
                              madhughṛtapragāḍhair ālepayet tāvad yāvat surūḍha iti surūḍhaṃ cainaṃ
                              punar vidhyet vidhānaṃ tu pūrvoktam eva || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.7"> tatra samyagviddham āmatailena pariṣecayet tryahāt
                              tryahāc ca vartiṃ sthūlatarāṃ dadyāt pariṣekaṃ ca tam eva || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.8"> atha vyapagatadoṣopadrave karṇe vardhanārthaṃ
                              laghuvardhanakaṃ kuryāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.9"> evaṃ vivardhitaḥ karṇaś chidyate tu dvidhā nṛṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               doṣato vā'bhighātād vā sandhānaṃ tasya me śṛṇu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.10"> tatra samāsena pañcadaśakarṇabandhākṛtayaḥ | tad
                              yathā nemisandhānaka utpalabhedyako vallūraka āsaṅgimo gaṇḍakarṇa
                              āhāryo nirvedhimo vyāyojimaḥ kapāṭasandhiko 'rdhakapāṭasandhikaḥ
                              saṃkṣipto hīnakarṇo vallīkarṇo yaṣṭikarṇaḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | teṣu
                              pṛthulāyatasamobhayapālir nemisandhānakaḥ vṛttāyatasamobhayapālir
                              utpalabhedyakaḥ hrasvavṛttasamobhayapālir vallūrakaḥ
                              abhyantaradīrghaikapālir āsaṅgimaḥ bāhya<pc> </pc>dīrghaikapālir
                              gaṇḍakarṇaḥ | apālir ubhayato 'py āhāryaḥ pīṭhopamapālir ubhayataḥ
                              kṣīṇaputrikāśrito nirvedhimaḥ | sthūlāṇusamaviṣamapālir vyāyojimaḥ |
                              abhyantaradīrghaikapālir itarālpapāliḥ | kapāṭasandhikaḥ
                              bāhyadīrghaikapālir itarālpapālir ardhakapāṭasandhikaḥ | tatra daśaite
                              karṇabandhavikalpāḥ sādhyāḥ teṣāṃ svanāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa
                              vyākhyātāḥ | saṃkṣiptādayaḥ pañcāsādhyāḥ | tatra śuṣkaśaṣkulir
                              utsannapālir itarālpapāliḥ saṃkṣiptaḥ anadhiṣṭhānapāliḥ paryantayoḥ
                              kṣīṇamāṃso hīnakarṇaḥ tanuviṣamālpapālir vallīkarṇaḥ
                              grathitamāṃsastabdhasirāsaṃtatasūkṣmapālir yaṣṭikarṇaḥ
                              nirmāṃsasaṃkṣiptāgrālpaśoṇitapāliḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | baddheṣv api tu
                                   śopha<pc> </pc>dāha<pc> </pc>rāga<pc> </pc>pāka<pc
                                   > </pc>piḍakā<pc> </pc>srāva<pc> </pc>yuktā na siddhim upayānti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.11"> bhavanti cātra |<anchor n="SS.1.16.11"/>
                              <caesura/>
                               yasya pālidvayam api karṇasya na bhaved iha |
                              <caesura/>
                               karṇapīṭhaṃ same madhye tasya viddhvā vivardhayet || </l>
                         <ab corresp="#SS.1.16.11" type="apparatus">
                              <list type="notes">
                                   <item corresp="#SS.1.16.11-n1">These verses in A (from
                                             <foreign>bhavanti cātra to śāstravit</foreign>) are
                                        absent from the Nepalese MSS and were probably absent in the
                                        version of the <emph>Suśrutasaṃhitā</emph> commented on by
                                        Cakrapāṇi, who cited them in his commentary as being "read
                                        by some" in regard to the joins
                                        (<foreign>sandhāna</foreign>) they describe.</item>
                              </list>
                         </ab>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.12"> bāhyāyām iha dīrghāyāṃ sandhir ābhyantaro bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               ābhyantarāyāṃ dīrghāyāṃ bāhyasandhir udāhṛtaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.13"> ekaiva tu bhavet pāliḥ sthūlā pṛthvī sthirā ca yā |
                              <caesura/>
                               tāṃ dvidhā pāṭayitvā tu chittvā copari sandhayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.14"> gaṇḍād utpāṭya māṃsena sānubandhena jīvatā |
                              <caesura/>
                               karṇapālīm āpāles tu kuryān nirlikhya śāstravit || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.15"> ato nyatamaṃ bandhaṃ cikīrṣur
                              agropaharaṇīyoktopasaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraṃ viśeṣataś cātropaharet surāmaṇḍaṃ
                              kṣīram udakaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ kapālacūrṇaṃ ceti | tato 'ṅganāṃ puruṣaṃ vā
                              grathitakeśāntaṃ laghubhuktavantam āptaiḥ suparigṛhītaṃ ca kṛtvā
                              bandham upadhārya chedyabhedyalekhyavyadhanair upapannair upapādya
                              karṇaśoṇitam avekṣya duṣṭam aduṣṭaṃ veti tatra vātaduṣṭe
                              dhānyāmloṣṇodakābhyāṃ pittaduṣṭe śītodakapayobhyāṃ śleṣmaduṣṭe
                              surāmaṇḍoṣṇodakābhyāṃ prakṣālya karṇau punar avalikhyānunnatam ahīnam
                              aviṣamaṃ ca karṇasandhiṃ sanniveśya sthitaraktaṃ sandadhyāt | tato
                              madhughṛtenābhyajya picuprotayor anyatareṇāvaguṇṭhya
                              sūtreṇānavagāḍhaman atiśithilaṃ ca baddhvā kapālacūrṇenāvakīryācārikam
                              upadiśed dvivraṇīyoktena ca vidhānenopacaret || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16"> bhavati cātra | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16x">vighaṭṭanaṃ divāsvapnaṃ vyāyāmam atibhojanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vyavāyam agnisaṃtāpaṃ vākśramaṃ ca vivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16.1"> (?āmatailaparīṣekaṃ trirātramavacārayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               tatas tailena saṃsṛṣṭaṃ tryahādapanayet picum ||) </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.17"> na cāśuddharaktam atipravṛttaraktaṃ kṣīṇaraktaṃ vā
                              saṃdadhyāt | sa hi vātaduṣṭe rakte rūḍho 'pi paripuṭanavān pittaduṣṭe
                              dāhapākarāgavedanāvān śleṣmaduṣṭe stabdhaḥ kaṇḍūmān atipravṛttarakte
                              śyāvaśophavān kṣīṇo 'lpamāṃso na vṛddhim upaiti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.18"> āmatailena trirātraṃ pariṣecayet trirātrāc ca picuṃ
                              parivartayet | sa yadā surūḍho nirupadravaḥ savarṇo bhavati tadainaṃ
                              śanaiś śanair abhivardhayet | ato 'nyathā
                              saṃrambhadāhapākarāgavedanāvān punaś chidyate vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.19"> athāsyāpraduṣṭasyābhivardhanārtham abhyaṅgaḥ | tad
                              yathā godhāpratudaviṣkirānūpaudakavasāmajjānau payaḥ sarpis tailaṃ
                              gaurasarṣapajaṃ ca yathālābhaṃ
                              saṃbhṛtyārkālarkabalātibalānantāpāmārgāśvagandhāvidārigandhākṣīraśuklājalaśūkamadhuravargapayasyāprativāpaṃ
                              tailaṃ vā pācayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.20"> sveditonmarditaṃ karṇaṃ snehenaitena yojayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               ato 'nupadravaḥ samyag balavāṃś ca vivardhate || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.21"> yavāśvagandhāyaṣṭyāhvais tilaiś codvartanaṃ hitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               śatāvaryaśvagandhābhyāṃ payasyair aṇḍajīvanaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.22"> tailaṃ vipakvaṃ sakṣīram abhyaṅgāt pālivardhanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               ye tu karṇā na vardhante svedasnehopapāditāḥ ||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23"> teṣām apāṅgadeśe tu kuryāt pracchānam eva tu |</l>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23b"> bāhyacchedaṃ na kurvīta vyāpadaḥ syus tato dhruvāḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.24"> baddhamātraṃ tu yaḥ karṇaṃ sahasaivābhivardhayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               āmakośī samādhmātaḥ kṣipram eva vimucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.25"> jātaromā suvartmā ca śliṣṭasandhiḥ samaḥ sthiraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               surūḍho 'vedano yaś ca taṃ karṇaṃ vardhayec chanaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.0"> amitāḥ karṇabandhās tu vijñeyāḥ kuśalair iha |
                              <caesura/>
                               yo yathā suviśiṣṭaḥ syāt taṃ tathā viniyojayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.1"> (karṇapālyāmayān nṝṇāṃ punar vakṣyāmi suśruta |
                              <caesura/>
                               karṇapalyāṃ prakupaitā vātapittakaphās trayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.2"> dvidhā vāpy atha saṃsṛṣṭāḥ kurvanti vividhā rujaḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               visphoṭaḥ stabdhatā śophaḥ pālyāṃ doṣe tu vātike || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.3"> dāhavisphoṭajananaṃ śophaḥ pākaś ca paittike |
                              <caesura/>
                               kaṇḍūḥ saśvayathuḥ stambho gurutvaṃ ca kaphātmake || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.4"> yathādoṣaṃ ca saṃśodhya kuryāt teṣāṃ cikitsitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               svedābhyaṅgaparīṣekaiḥ pralepāsṛgvimokṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.5"> mṛdvīṃ kriyāṃ bṛṃhaṇīyair yathāsvaṃ bhojanais
                              tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               ya evaṃ vetti doṣāṇāṃ cikitsāṃ kartum arhati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.6"> ata ūrdhvaṃ nāmaliṅgair vakṣye pālyām upadravān |
                              <caesura/>
                               atpāṭakaś cotpuṭakaḥ śyāvaḥ kaṇḍūyuto bhṛśam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.7"> avamanthaḥ sakaṇḍūko granthiko jambulas tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               srāvī ca dāhavāṃś caiva śṛṇveṣāṃ kramaśaḥ kriyām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.8"> apāmārgaḥ sarjarasaḥ pāṭalālakucatvacau |
                              <caesura/>
                               utpāṭake pralepaḥ syāt tailam ebhiś ca pācayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.9"> śampākaśigrupūtīkān godhāmedo 'tha tadvasām |
                              <caesura/>
                               vārāhaṃ gavyam aiṇeyaṃ pittaṃ sarpiś ca saṃsṛjet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.10"> lepam utpuṭake dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               gaurīṃ sugandhāṃ saśyāmām anantāṃ taṇḍulīyakam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.11"> śyāve pralepanaṃ dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               pāṭhāṃ rasāñjanaṃ kṣaudraṃ tathā syād uṣṇakāñjikam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.12"> dadyāl lepaṃ sakaṇḍūke tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               vraṇībhūtasya deyaṃ syād idaṃ tailaṃ vijānatā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.13"> madhukakṣīrakākolījīvakādyair vipācitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               godhāvarāhasarpāṇāṃ vasāḥ syuḥ kṛtabṛṃhaṇe || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.14"> pralepanam idaṃ dadyād avasicyāvamanthake |
                              <caesura/>
                               prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ samaṅgāṃ dhavam eva ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.15"> tailam ebhiś ca saṃpakvaṃ śṛṇu kaṇḍūmataḥ kriyām
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               sahadevā viśvadevā ajākṣīraṃ sasaindhavam |
                              <caesura/>
                               etair ālepanaṃ dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.16"> granthike guṭikāṃ pūrvaṃ srāvayed avapāṭya tu |
                              <caesura/>
                               tataḥ saindhavacūrṇaṃ tu ghṛṣṭvā lepaṃ pradāpayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.17"> likhitvā tatsrutaṃ ghṛṣṭvā cūrṇair lodhrasya
                              jambule |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣīreṇa pratisāryainaṃ śuddhaṃ saṃropayet tataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.18"> madhuparṇī madhūkaṃ ca ma madhukaṃ madhunā saha
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               lepaḥ srāviṇi dātavyas tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.19"> pañcavalkaiḥ samadhukaiḥ piṣṭais taiś ca
                              ghṛtānvitaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               jīvakādyaiḥ sasarpiṣkair dahyamānaṃ pralepayet ||) </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.27"> viśleṣitāyās tv atha nāsikāyā
                              <caesura/>
                               vakṣyāmi sandhānavidhiṃ yathāvat |
                              <caesura/>
                               nāsāpramāṇaṃ pṛthivīruhāṇāṃ
                              <caesura/>
                               patraṃ gṛhītvā tv avalambi tasya || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.28"> tena pramāṇena hi gaṇḍapārśvād
                              <caesura/>
                               utkṛtya baddhaṃ tv atha nāsikāgram |
                              <caesura/>
                               vilikhya cāśu pratisaṃdadhīta
                              <caesura/>
                               tat sādhubandhair bhiṣag apramattaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.29"> susaṃhitaṃ samyag ato yathāvan
                              <caesura/>
                               nāḍīdvayenābhisamīkṣya baddhvā |
                              <caesura/>
                               pronnamya cainām avacūrṇayet tu
                              <caesura/>
                               pataṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāñjanaiś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.30">saṃchādya samyak picunā sitena
                              <caesura/>
                               tailena siñced asakṛt tilānām |
                              <caesura/>
                               ghṛtaṃ ca pāyyaḥ sa naraḥ sujīrṇe
                              <caesura/>
                               snigdho virecyaḥ sa yathopadeśam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.31">rūḍhaṃ ca sandhānam upāgataṃ syāt
                              <caesura/>
                               tad ardhaśeṣaṃ tu punar nikṛntet |
                              <caesura/>
                               hīnāṃ punar vardhayituṃ yateta
                              <caesura/>
                               samāṃ ca kuryād ativṛddhamāṃsām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.16.32"> nāḍīyogaṃ vinauṣṭhasya nāsāsandhānavad vidhim |
                              <caesura/>
                               ya evam eva jānīyāt sa rājñaḥ kartum arhati || </l>

                         <trailer xml:id="SS.1.16.colophon">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              karṇavyadhabandhavidhirnāma ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </trailer>
                    </div>


                    <div n="17" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.1"> athāta āmapakvaiṣaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.3"> śophasamutthānā granthividradhyalajīprabhṛtayaḥ
                              prāyeṇa vyādhayo 'bhihitā anekākṛtayaḥ tair vilakṣaṇaḥ pṛthurgrathitaḥ
                              samo viṣamo vā tvaṅnāṃsasthāyī doṣasaṃghātaḥ śarīraikadeśotthitaḥ
                              śopha ity ucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.4"> sa ṣaḍvidho
                              vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātāgantunimittaḥ | tasya doṣarūpavyañjanair
                              lakṣaṇāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra vātaśopho 'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā paruṣo
                              mṛduranavasthitāstodāyaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti pittaśophaḥ pīto
                              mṛduḥ sarakto vā śīghrānusāryoṣādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti
                              śleṣmaśophaḥ pāṇḍuḥ śuklo vā kaṭhinaḥ śitaḥ snigdho mandānusārī
                              kaṇḍvādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti sarvavarṇavedanaḥ sannipātajaḥ
                              pittavacchoṇitajo 'tikṛṣṇaś ca pittaraktalakṣaṇa āganturlohitāvabhāsaś
                              ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.5"> sa yadā bāhyābhyantaraiḥ kriyāviśeṣair na
                              saṃbhāvitaḥ praśamayituṃ kriyāviparyayādbahutvād vā doṣāṇāṃ tadā
                              pākābhimukho bhavati | tasyāmsya pacyamānasya pakvasya ca
                              lakṣaṇamucyamānam upadhāraya | tatra mandoṣmatā tvaksavarṇatā
                              śītaśophatā sthairyaṃ mandavedanatā'lpaśophatā cāmalakṣaṇamuddiṣṭaṃ
                              sūcibhir iva nistudyate daśyata iva pipīlikābhis tābhiś ca saṃsarpyata
                              iva chidyata iva śastreṇa bhidyata iva śaktibhis tāḍyata iva daṇḍena
                              pīḍyata iva pāṇinā ghaṭyata iva cāṅgulyā dahyate pacyata iva
                              cāgnikṣārābhyāṃ oṣacoṣaparīdāhāś ca bhavanti vṛś cikaviddha iva ca
                              sthānāsanaśayaneṣu na śāntim upaiti ādhmātabastirivātataś ca śopho
                              bhavati tvagvaivarṇyaṃ śophābhivṛddhirjvaradāhapipāsā bhaktāruciś ca
                              pacyamānaliṅgaṃ vedanopaśāntiḥ pāṇḍutā'lpaśophatā
                              valīprādurbhāvastvakparipuṭanaṃ nimnadarśanamaṅgulyā'vapīḍite
                              pratyunnamanaṃ bastāvivodakasaṃcaraṇaṃ pūyasya
                              prapīḍayatyekamantamante vā'vapīḍite muhurmuhustodaḥ kaṇḍūrunnatatā
                              vyādherupadravaśāntirbhaktābhikāṅkṣā ca pakvaliṅgam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.6"> kaphajeṣu tu rogeṣu gambhīragatitvād abhighātajeṣu
                              vā keṣucid asamastaṃ pakvalakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā pakvam apakvam iti manyamāno
                              bhiṣaṅnoham upaiti | yatra hi tvaksavarṇatā śītaśophatā
                              sthaulyamalparujatā'śmavac ca ghanatā na tatra moham upeyād iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.7"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               āmaṃ vipacyamānaṃ ca samyak pakvaṃ ca yo bhiṣak |
                              <caesura/>
                               jānīyāt sa bhaved vaidyaḥ śeṣās taskaravṛttayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.8"> vātādṛte nāsti rujā na pākaḥ pittādṛte nāsti kaphāc
                              ca pūyaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmāt samastāḥ paripākakāle pacanti śophāṃs traya eva doṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.8ef"/>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.8gh"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.9"> kālāntareṇābhyuditaṃ tu pittaṃ kṛtvā vaśe vātakaphau
                              prasahya |
                              <caesura/>
                               pacaty ataḥ śoṇitam eva pāko mato 'pareṣāṃ viduṣāṃ dvitīyaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.9ef"/>
                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.9gh"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.10"> tatra āmacchede māṃsasirāsnāyvasthisandhivyāpādanam
                              atimātraṃ śoṇitātipravṛttir vedanāprādurbhāvo 'vadaraṇam
                              anekopadravadarśanaṃ kṣatavidradhirvā bhavati | sa yadā bhayamohābhyāṃ
                              pakvam apy apakvam iti manyamānaś ciram upekṣate vyādhiṃ vaidyas tadā
                              gambhīrānugato dvāram alabhamānaḥ pūyaḥ svam āśrayam
                              avadā(ā.dī)ryotasaṅgaṃ mahāntam avakāśaṃ kṛtvā nāḍīṃ janayitvā
                              kṛcchrasādhyo bhavaty asādhyo veti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.11"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               yaś chinatty āmam ajñānād yaś ca pakvam upekṣate |
                              <caesura/>
                               śvapacāv iva mantavyau tāv aniścitakāriṇau || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.12"> prāk śastrakarmaṇaś ceṣṭaṃ bhojayed āturaṃ bhiṣak |
                              <caesura/>
                               madyapaṃ pāyayen madyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yo vedanāsahaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.13"> na mūrcchaty annasaṃyogān mattaḥ śastraṃ na
                              budhyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmād avaśyaṃ bhoktavyaṃ rogeṣūkteṣu karmaṇi || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.14"> prāṇo hy ābhyantaro nṇṇāṃ bāhyaprāṇaguṇānvitaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhārayaty avirodhena śarīraṃ pāñcabhautikam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.15"> alpo mahān vā kriyayā vinā yaḥ samucchritaḥ pākam
                              upaiti śophaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               viśālamūlo viṣamo vidagdhaḥ sa kṛcchritāṃ yāty avagāḍhadoṣaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.16"> ālepavisrāvaṇaśodhanais tu samyak prayukair yadi
                              nopaśāmyet |
                              <caesura/>
                               pacyet śīghraṃ samam alpamūlaḥ sa piṇḍitaś copari connataḥ syāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.17"> kakṣaṃ samāsādya yathaiva vahnir vāte(ā.yvī)ritaḥ
                              saṃdahati prasahya |
                              <caesura/>
                               tathaiva pūyo 'py aviniḥsṛto hi māṃsaṃ sirāḥ snāyu ca khādatīha || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.18"> ādau vimlāpanaṃ kuryād dvitīyam avasecanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               tṛtīyam upanāhaṃ tu caturthīṃ pāṭanakriyām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.17.19"> pañcamaṃ śodhanaṃ kuryāt ṣaṣṭhaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               ete kramā vraṇasyoktāḥ saptamaṃ vaikṛtāpaham || </l>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne āmapakvaiṣaṇīyo 'nāma
                              saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="18" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.1"> athāto vraṇālepanabandhavidhim adhyāyaṃ
                              vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.3"> ālipa ādya upakramaḥ eṣa sarvaśophānāṃ sāmānyaḥ
                              pradhānatamaś ca taṃ ca pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tato bandhaḥ pradhānaṃ
                              tena śuddhirvraṇaropaṇamasthisaṃdhisthairyaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.4"> tatra pratilomamālimpennānulomam | pratilome hi
                              samyagauṣadhamavatiṣṭhate 'nupraviśati romakūpān svedavāhibhiś ca
                              sirāmukhairvīryaṃ prāpnoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.5"> na ca śuṣyamāṇamupekṣeta anyatra pīḍayitavyāt śuṣko
                              hy apārthako rukkaraś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.6"> sa trividhaḥ pralepaḥ pradeha ālepaś ca | teṣām
                              antaraṃ pralepaḥ śītas tanur aviśoṣī viśoṣī ca pradehas tūṣṇaḥ śīto vā
                              bahalo 'bahur aviśoṣī ca madhaymo 'trālepaḥ | tatra
                              raktapittaprasādakṛd ālepaḥ pradeho vātaśleṣmapraśamanaḥ saṃdhānaḥ
                              śodhano ropaṇaḥ śophavedanāpahaś ca tasyopayogaḥ kṣatākṣateṣu yas tu
                              kṣateṣūpayujyate sa bhūyaḥ kalka iti saṃjñāṃ labhate
                              niruddālepanasaṃjñaḥ tenāsrāvasannirodho mṛdutā pūtimāṃsāpakarṣaṇam
                              anantardoṣatā vraṇaśuddhiś ca bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.7"> avidagdheṣu śopheṣu hitam ālepanaṃ bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               yathāsvaṃ doṣaśamanaṃ dāhakaṇḍūrujāpaham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.8"> tvakprasādanam evāgryaṃ māṃsaraktaprasādanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               dāhapraśamanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ todakaṇḍūvināśanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.9"> marmadeśeṣu ye togā guhyeṣv api tathā nṛām |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃśodhanāya teṣāṃ hi kuryād ālepanaṃ bhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.10"> (?ṣaḍbhāgaṃ paittike snehaṃ catrubhāgaṃ tu vātike |
                              <caesura/>
                               aṣṭabhāgaṃ tu kaphaje snehamātrāṃ pradāpayet ||) </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.11"> tasya pramāṇamārdramāhiṣacarmotsedham upadiśanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.12"> na cālepaṃ rātrau prayuñjīta mābhūc
                              chaityapihitoṣmaṇas tad anirgamād vikārapravṛtti(ā.ddhi)r iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.13"> pradehasādhye vyādhau tu hitam ālepanaṃ divā |
                              <caesura/>
                               pittaraktābhighātotthe saviṣe ca viśeṣataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.14"> na ca paryuṣitaṃ lepaṃ kadācidavacārayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               uparyupari lepaṃ tu na kadācit pradāpayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.15"> ūṣmāṇaṃ vedanāṃ dāhaṃ ghanatvājjanayet sa hi |
                              <caesura/>
                               na ca tenaiva lepena pradehaṃ dāpayet punaḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.15ef"> śuṣkabhāvāt sa nirvīryo yukto 'pi syād apārthakaḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.16"> ata ūrdhvaṃ vraṇabandhanadravyāṇy upadekṣyāmaḥ tad
                              yathā
                              kṣaumakārpāsāvikadukūlakauśeyapatrorṇacīnapaṭṭacarmāntarvalkalālābūśakalalatāvidalarajjutūlaphalasantānikālauhānīti
                              teṣaṃ vyādhiṃ kālaṃ cāvekṣyopayogaḥ prakaraṇataś caiṣām ādeśaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.17"> tatra
                              kośadāmasvastikānuvellitapra(ā.mu)tolīmaṇḍalasthagikāyamakakhaṭvācīnavibandhavitānagophaṇāḥ
                              pañcāṅgī ceti caturdaśa bandhaviśeṣāḥ | teṣāṃ nāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ
                              prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.18"> tatra kośamaṅguṣṭhāṅguliparvasu vidadhyāt
                              dāmasaṃbādhe 'ṅge sandhikūrcakabhrūstanāntaratalakarṇeṣu svastikaṃ
                              anuvellitaṃ tu śākhāsu grīvāmeḍhrayoḥ pratolīṃ vṛtte 'ṅge maṇḍalaṃ
                              aṅguṣṭhāṅgulimeḍhrāgreṣu sthagikāṃ yamalavraṇayor yamakaṃ
                              hanuśaṅkhagaṇḍeṣu khaṭvāṃ apāṅgayoś cīnaṃ pṛṣṭhodaroraḥsu vibandhaṃ
                              mūrdhani vitānaṃ cibukanāsauṣṭhāṃsabastiṣu gophaṇāṃ jatruṇa ūrdhvaṃ
                              pañcāṅgīm iti yo vā yasmin śarīrapradeśe suniviṣṭo bhavati taṃ tasmin
                              vidadhyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.19"> yantraṇam ūrdhvamadhistiryak ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.20"> tatra ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ dattvā
                              vāmahastaparikṣepamṛjum anāviddham asaṃkucitaṃ mṛdu paṭṭaṃ niveśya
                              badhnīyāt | na ca vraṇasyopari kuryād granthim ābādhakaraṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.21"> na ca vikeśikauṣadhe 'tisnigdhe 'tirūkṣe viṣame vā
                              kurvīta yasmād atisnehāt kledo raukṣyāc chedo
                              durnyāsāhraṇavartmāvagharṣaṇam iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.22"> tatra vraṇayatanaviśeṣād bandhaviśeṣas trividho
                              bhavati gāḍhaḥ samaḥ śithila iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.23"> pīḍayann arujo gāḍhaḥ socchvāsaḥ śithilaḥ smṛtaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               naiva gāḍho na śithilaḥ samo bandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.24"> tatra sphikkukṣikakṣāvaṅkṣaṇoruśiraḥsu gāḍhaḥ
                              śākhāvadanakarṇakaṇṭhameḍhramuṣkapṛṣṭhapārśvodaroraḥsu samaḥ akṣṇoḥ
                              sandhiṣu ca śithila ti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.25"> tatra paittikaṃ gāḍhasthāne samaṃ badhnīyāt
                              samasthāne śithilaṃ śithilasthāne naiva evaṃ śoṇitaduṣṭaṃ ca
                              ślaiṣmikaṃ śithilasthāne samaṃ samasthāne gāḍhaṃ gāḍhasthāne
                              gāḍhataraṃ evaṃ vātaduṣṭaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.26"> tatra paittikaṃ śaradi grīṣme dvirahno badhnīyāt
                              raktopadrutamapyevaṃ ślaiṣmikaṃ hemantavasantayostryahāt
                              vātopadrutamapyevam | evamabhyūhya bandhaviparyayaṃ ca kuryāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.27"> tatra samaśithilasthāneṣu gāḍhaṃ baddhe
                              vikeśikauṣadhanair arthakyaṃ śophavedanāprādurbhāvaś ca
                              gāḍhasamasthāneṣu śithilaṃ baddhe vikeśikauṣadhapatanaṃ
                              paṭṭasaṃcārāhraṇavartmāvagharṣanam iti gāḍhaśithilasthāneṣu samaṃ
                              baddhe ca guṇābhāva iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.28"> aviparītabandhe vedanopaśāntir asṛkprasādo mārdavaṃ
                              ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.29"> abadhyamāno
                              daṃśamaśakatṛṇakāṣṭhopalapāṃśuśītavātātapaprabhṛtibhir viśeṣair
                              abhihanyate vraṇo vividhavedanopadrutaś ca duṣṭatām upaity ālepanādīni
                              cāsya viśoṣam upayānti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.30"> cūrṇitaṃ mathitaṃ bhagnaṃ viśliṣṭam atipātitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               asthisnāyusirācchinnam āśu bandhena rohati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.31"> sukham evaṃ vraṇī śete sukhaṃ gacchati tiṣṭhati |
                              <caesura/>
                               sukhaṃ śayyāsanasthasya kṣipraṃ saṃrohati vraṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.32"> abandhyāḥ pittaraktābhighātaviṣanimittā yadā ca
                              śophadāhapākarāgatodavedanābhibhūtāḥ kṣārāgnidagdhāḥ pākāt
                              prakuthitapraśīrṇamāṃsāś ca bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.33"> kuṣṭhinām agnidagdhānāṃ piḍakā madhumehinām |
                              <caesura/>
                               karṇikāś conduruviṣe viṣajuṣṭavraṇāś ca ye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.34"> māṃsāpāke na badhyante gudapāke ca dāruṇe |
                              <caesura/>
                               svabuddhyā cāpi vibhajet kṛtyākṛtyāṃś ca buddhimān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.35"> deśaṃ doṣaṃ ca vijñāya vraṇaṃ ca vraṇakovidaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ṛtūṃś ca parisaṃkhyāya tato bandhān niveśayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.36"> ūrdhvaṃ tiryag adhastāc ca yantraṇā trividhā smṛtā
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               yathā ca badhyate bandhas tathā vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.37"> ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ dattvā mṛdu caivāpi paṭṭakam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vikeśikāmauṣadhaṃ ca nātisnigdhaṃ samācaret || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.38"> prakledayatyatisnigdhā tathā rūkṣā kṣiṇoti ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               yuktasnehā ropayati durnyastā vartma gharṣati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.39"> viṣamaṃ ca vraṇaṃ kuryāt stambhayet srāvayet tathā
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               yathāvraṇaṃ viditvā tu yogaṃ vaidyaḥ prayojayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.40"> pittaje raktaje vā'pi sakṛteva parikṣipet |
                              <caesura/>
                               asakṛt kaphaje vā'pi vātaje ca vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.41"> talena pratipīḍyātha srāvayed anulomataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sarvāṃś ca bandhān gūḍhāntān sandhīṃś ca viniveśayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.42"> oṣṭhasyāpyeṣa sandhāne yathoddiṣṭo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               buddhyotprekṣyābhiyuktena tathā cāsthiṣu jānatā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.43"> uttiṣṭhato niṣaṇṇasya śayanaṃ vā'dhigacchataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               gacchato vividhair yānair nāsya duṣyati sa vraṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.44"> ye ca syur māṃsasaṃsthā vai tvaggatāś ca tathā
                              vraṇāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sandhyasthikoṣṭhaprāptāś ca sirāsnāyugatās tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.18.45"> tathā'vagāḍhagambhīrāḥ sarvato viṣamasthitāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               naite sādhayituṃ śakyā ṛte bandhādbhavanti hi || </l>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              vraṇālepanabandhavidhirnāmāṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>





                    </div>


                    <div n="19" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>ekonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.1"> athāto vraṇitopāsanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantriḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.3"> vraṇitasya prathamamevāgāramanvicchet taccāgāraṃ
                              praśastavāstvād ikaṃ karyam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.4"> praśastavāstuni gṛhe śucāvātapavarjite |
                              <caesura/>
                               nivāte na ca rogāḥ syuḥ śārīrāgantumānasāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.5"> tasmin śayanamasaṃbādhaṃ svāstīrṇaṃ manojñaṃ
                              prākśiraskaṃ saśastraṃ kurvīt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.6"> sukhaceṣṭāpracāraḥ syāt svāstīrṇe śayane vraṇī |
                              <caesura/>
                               prācyāṃ diśi sthitā devāstatpūjārthaṃ ca tacchiraḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.7"> tasmin suhṛdbhir anukūlaiḥ priyaṃvadair upāsyamāno
                              yatheṣṭamāsīt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.8"> suhṛdo vikṣipantyāśu kathābhir vraṇavedanāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               āśvāsayanto bahuśastvanukūlāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.9"> na ca divānidrāvaśagaḥ syāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.10"> divāsvapnāddraṇe kaṇḍūrgātrāṇāṃ gauravaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               śvayathurvedanā rāgaḥ srāvaś caiva bhṛśaṃ bhavet ||// </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.11"> utthānasaṃveśanaparivartanacaṅkramaṇoccair
                              bhāṣaṇādyāsvātmaceṣṭāsvapramatto vraṇaṃ saṃrakṣet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.12"> sthānāsanaṃ caṅkramaṇaṃ divāsvapnaṃ tathaiva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               vraṇito na niṣeveta śaktimān api mānavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.13"> utthānādyāsanaṃ sthānaṃ śayyā cātiniṣevitā |
                              <caesura/>
                               prāpnuyānmārutādaṅge rujastasmād vivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.14"> gamyānāṃ ca strīṇāṃ
                              saṃdarśanasaṃbhāṣaṇasaṃsparśanāni dūrataḥ pariharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.15"> strīdarśanādibhiḥ śukraṃ kadāciccalitaṃ sravet |
                              <caesura/>
                               grāmyadharmakṛtāndoṣān so 'saṃsarge 'pyavāpnuyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.16">
                              navadhānyamāṣatilakalāyakulatthaniṣpāvaharitakaśākāmlalavaṇakaṭukaguḍapiṣṭavikṛtivallūraśuṣkaśākājāvikānūpaudakamāṃsavasāśītodakakṛśarāpāyasadadhidugdhatakraprabhṛtīn
                              pariharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.17"> takrānto navadhānyādiryo 'yaṃ varga udāhṛtaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               doṣasaṃjanano hyeṣa vijñeyaḥ pūyavardhanaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.18"> madyapaś ca maireyāriṣṭāsavaśīdhusurāvikārān
                              pariharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.19"> madyamamlaṃ tathā rūkṣaṃ tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ ca vīryataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               āśukāri ca tat pītaṃ kṣipraṃ vyāpādayed draṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.20">
                              vātātaparajodhūmāvaśyāyātisevanātibhojanāniṣṭabhojanāśravaṇadarśanerṣyāmarṣabhayakrodhaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇaviṣamāśanaśayanopavāsavāgvyāyāmasthānacaṅkramaṇaśītavātaviruddhādhyaśanājīrṇamakṣikādyā
                              bādhāḥ pariharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.21"> vraṇinaḥ saṃprataptasya kāraṇair evam ādibhiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣīṇaśoṇitamāṃsasya bhuktaṃ samyaṅga jīryati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.22"> ajīrṇāt pavanādīnāṃ vibhramo balavān bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               tataḥ śopharujāsrāvadāhapākānavāpnuyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.23"> sadā nīcanakharomṇā śucinā śuklavāsasā
                              śāntimaṅgaladevatābrāhmaṇagurupareṇa bhavitavyam iti | tat kasya hetoḥ
                              hiṃsāvihārāṇi hi mahāvīryāṇi rakṣāṃsi paśupatikuberakumārānucarāṇi
                              māṃsaśoṇitapriyatvāt kṣatajanimittaṃ vraṇinam upasarpanti satkārārthaṃ
                              jighāṃsūni vā kadācit || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.24"> bhavati cātra
                              <caesura/>
                               teṣāṃ satkārakāmānāṃ prayatetāntarātmanā |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhūpabalyupahārāṃś ca bhakṣyāṃś caivopahārayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.25"> te tu saṃtarpitā ātmavantamk na hiṃsyuḥ | tasmāt
                              satatamatandrito janaparivṛto nityaṃ
                              dīpodakaśastrasragdāmapuṣpalājādyalaṅkṛte veśmani sāṃpanmaṅgalamano
                              'nukūlāḥ kathāḥ śṛṇvannāsīta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.26"> saṃpadādyanukūlābhiḥ kathābhiḥ prītamānasaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               āśāvān vyādhimokṣāya kṣipraṃ sukhamavāpnuyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.27"> ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvavedābhihitair aparaiś
                              cāśīrvidhānair upādhyāyā bhiṣajaś ca sandhyayo rakṣāṃ kuryuḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.28"> sarṣapāriṣṭapatrābhyāṃ sarpiṣā lavaṇena ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               dvirahnaḥ kārayed dhūpaṃ daśarātramatandritaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.29"> chatrāmaticchatrāṃ lāṅgū(ā.ṅga)līṃ jaṭilāṃ
                              brahmacāriṇīṃ lakṣmīṃ guhāmatiguhāṃ vacāmativiṣāṃ śatavīryāṃ
                              sahasravīryāṃ siddhārthakāṃś ca śirasā dhārayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.30"> vyajyeta bālavyajanair vraṇaṃ na ca vighaṭṭayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               na tuden na ca kaṇḍūyec chayānaḥ paripālayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.31"> anena vidhinā yuktam ādāv eva niśācarāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               vanaṃ keśāriṇā+ākrāntaṃ varjayanti mṛgā iva || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.32"> jīrṇaśālyodanaṃ snigdhamalpamuṣṇaṃ dravottaram |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhuñjāno jāṅgalair māṃsaiḥ śīghraṃ vraṇam apohati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.33"> taṇḍulīyakajīvantīsuniṣaṇṇakavāstukaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               bālamūlakavātārkapaṭolaiḥ kāravellakaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.34"> sadāḍimaiḥ sāmalakair ghṛtabhṛṣṭaiḥ sasaindhavaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               anyair evaṃguṇair vā'pi mudgādīnāṃ rasena vā ||
                              <caesura/>
                               śaktūn vilepīṃ kulmāṣaṃ jalaṃ cāpi śṛtaṃ pibet | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.35"> divā na nidrāvaśago nivātagṛhagocaraḥ ||
                              <caesura/>
                               vraṇī vaidyavaśe tiṣṭhan śīghraṃ vraṇamapohati | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.36"> vraṇe śvayathurāyāsāt sa ca rāgaś ca jāgarāt |
                              <caesura/>
                               tau ca ruk ca divāsvāpāt tāś ca mṛtyuś ca maithunāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.19.37"> evaṃvṛttasamācāro vraṇī saṃpadyate sukhī |
                              <caesura/>
                               āyuś ca dīrgham āpnoti dhanvantarivaco yathā || </l>

                         <p ana="trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vraṇitopāsanīyo
                              namaikonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
