                    <div n="20" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> viṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.1"> athāto hitāhitīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.3"> yadvāyoḥ pathyaṃ tat pittasyāpathyam ity anena
                              hetunā na kiṃcid dravyam ekāntena hitam ahitaṃ vā'stīti kecid ācāryā
                              bruvate | tat tu na samyak | iha khalu yasmād dravyāṇi svabhāvataḥ
                              saṃyogataś caikāntahitāny ekāntāhitāni hitāhitāni ca bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.4"> tatra ekāntahitāni jātisātmyāt
                              salilaghṛtadugdhaudanaprabhṛtīni ekāntāhitāni tu
                              dahanapacanamāraṇādiṣu pravṛttānyagnikṣāraviṣādīni saṃyogādaparāṇi
                              viṣatulyāni bhavanti hitāhitāni tu yadvāyoḥ pathyaṃ tatpittasyāpathyam
                              iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.5"> ataḥ sarvaprāṇināmayamāhārārthaṃ varga upadiśyate
                              tad yathā
                              raktaśaliṣaṣṭikakaṅgukamukundakapāṇḍukapītakapramodakakālakāsanapuṣpakakardamakaśakunāhṛtasugandhakakalamanīvārakodravoddālakaśyāmākagodhūmaveṇuyavādaya
                              eṇahariṇakuraṅgamṛgamātṛkāśvadaṃṣṭrākarālakrakarakapotalāvatittirikapiñjalavartīravartikādīnāṃ
                              māṃsāni
                              mudgavanamudgamakuṣṭhakalāyamasūramaṅgalyacaṇakahareṇvāḍhakīsatīnāḥ
                              cillivāstukasuniṣaṇṇakajīvantītaṇḍulīyakamaṇḍūkaparṇyaḥ gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ
                              saindhavadāḍimāmalakam ity eṣa vargaḥ sarvaprāṇināṃ sāmānyataḥ
                              pathyatamaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.6"> tathā
                              brahmacaryanivātaśayanoṣṇodakasnānaniśāsvapnavyāyāmāś caikāntataḥ
                              pathyatamāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.7"> ekāntahitānyekāntāhitāni ca prāgupadiṣṭāni
                              hitāhitāni tu yadvāyoḥ pathyaṃ tatpittasyāpathyam iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.8"> saṃyogatastvaparāṇi viṣatulyāni bhavanti | tad yathā
                              vallīphalakavakakarīrāmlaphalalavaṇakulatthapiṇyākadadhitailavirohipiṣṭaśuṣkaśākājāvikamāṃsamadyajāmbavacilicimamatsyagodhāvarāhāṃś
                              ca naikadhyamaśnīyāt payasā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.9"> rogaṃ sātmyaṃ ca deśaṃ ca kālaṃ dehaṃ ca buddhimān |
                              <caesura/>
                               avekṣyāgnyādikān bhāvān rogavṛtteḥ prayojayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.10ab"> avasthāntarabāhulyādrogādīnāṃ vyavasthitam | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.10cd"> dravyaṃ necchanti bhiṣaja icchanti svastharakṣaṇe
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.11"> dvayor anyatarādāne vadanti viṣadugdhayoḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dugdhasyaikāntahitatāṃ viṣamekāntato 'hitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.12"> evaṃ yuktaraseṣveṣu dravyeṣu salilādiṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               ekāntahitatāṃ viddhi vatsa suśrta nānyathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.13"> ato 'nyāny api saṃyogādahitāni vakṣyāmaḥ na
                              vavirūḍhadhānyair vasāmadhupayoguḍamāṣair vā grāmyānūpaudakapiśitādīni
                              nābhyavaharet na payomadhubhyāṃ rohiṇīśākaṃ jātukaśākaṃ vā'śnīyāt
                              balākāṃ vāruṇīkulmāṣābhyāṃ kākamācīṃ pippalīmaricābhyāṃ
                              nāḍībhaṅgaśākakukkuṭadadhīni ca naikadhyaṃ madhu coṣṇodakānupānaṃ
                              pittena cāmamāṃsāni surākṛśarāpāyasāṃś ca naikadhyaṃ sauvīrakeṇa saha
                              tilaśaṣkulīṃ matsyaiḥ sahekṣuvikārān guḍena kākamācīṃ madhunā mūlakaṃ
                              guḍena vārāhaṃ madhunā ca saha viruddhaṃ kṣīreṇa
                              mūlakamāmrajāmbavaśvāvicchūkaragodhāś ca sarvāṃś ca matsyān payasā
                              viśeṣeṇa cilicimaṃ kadalīphalaṃ tālaphalena payasā dadhnā takreṇa vā
                              lakucaphalaṃ payasā dadhnā māṣasūpena vā prāk payasaḥ payaso 'nte vā
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.14"> ataḥ karmaviruddhān vakṣyāmaḥ kapotān
                              sarṣapatailabhṛṣṭānnādyāt kapiñjalamayūralāvatittirigodhāś
                              cairaṇḍadārvyagnisiddhā eraṇḍatailasiddhā vā nādyāt kāṃsyabhājane
                              daśarātraparyuṣitaṃ sarpiḥ madhu coṣṇair uṣṇe vā matsyaparipacane
                              śrṇgaveraparipacane vā siddhāṃ kākamācīṃ tilakalkasiddhamupodikāśākaṃ
                              nārikelena varāhavasā paribhṛṣṭāṃ balākāṃ bhāsamaṅgāraśūlyaṃ nāśnīyād
                              iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.15"> ato mānaviruddhān vakṣyāmaḥ madhvambunī
                              madhusarpiṣī mānatastulye nāśnīyāt snehau madhusnehau jalasnehau vā
                              viśeṣādāntarīkṣodakānupānau || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.16"> ata ūrdhvaṃ rasadvandvāni rasato vīryato vipākataś
                              ca viruddhāni vakṣyāmaḥ tatra madhurāmlau rasavīryaviruddhau
                              madhuralavaṇau ca madhurakaṭukau ca sarvataḥ madhuratiktau
                              rasavipākābhyāṃ madhurakaṣāyau ca amlalavaṇau rasataḥ amlakaṭukau
                              rasavipākābhyāṃ amlatiktāvamlakaṣāyau ca sarvataḥ lavaṇakaṭukau
                              rasavipākābhyāṃ lavaṇatiktau lavaṇakaṣāyau ca sarvataḥ kaṭutiktau
                              rasavīryābhyāṃ kaṭukaṣāyau ca tiktakaṣāyau rasataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.17"> taratamayogayuktāṃś ca
                              bhāvānatirūkṣānatisnigdhānatyuṣṇānatiśītānity evam ādīn vivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.18"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               viruddhāny evam ādīni vīryato yāni kāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               tāny ekāntāhitāny eva śeṣaṃ vidyād dhitāhitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.19"> vyādhim indriyadaurbalyaṃ maraṇaṃ cādhigacchati |
                              <caesura/>
                               viruddharasavīryāṇi bhuñjāno 'nātmavān naraḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.20"> yat kiṃcid doṣam utkleśya bhuktaṃ kāyānna nirharet
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               rasādiṣv ayathārthaṃ vā tad vikārāya kalpate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.21"> viruddhāśanajān rogān pratihanti virecanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vamanaṃ śamanaṃ vā'pi pūrvaṃ vā hitasevanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.22"> sātymyato 'lpatayā vā'pi dīptāgnestaruṇasya ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               snigdhavyāyāmabalināṃ viruddhaṃ vitathaṃ bhavet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.23"> atha vātaguṇān vakṣyāmaḥ
                              <caesura/>
                               pūrvaḥ samadhuraḥ snigdho lavaṇaś caiva mārutaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               gururvidāhajanano raktapittābhivardhanaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.24"> kṣatānāṃ viṣajuṣṭānāṃ vraṇinaḥ śleṣmalāś ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               teṣām eva viśeṣeṇa sadā rogavivardhanaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.25"> vātalānāṃ praśastaś ca śrāntānāṃ kaphaśoṣiṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               teṣām eva viśeṣeṇa vraṇakledavivardhanaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.26"> madhuraś cāvidāhī ca kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dakṣiṇo mārutaḥ śreṣṭhaś cakṣuṣyo balavardhanaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.27"> raktapittapraśamano na ca vātaprakopaṇaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               viśado rūkṣaparuṣaḥ kharaḥ snehabalāpahaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.28"> paścimo mārutastīkṣṇaḥ kaphamedoviśoṣaṇaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sadyaḥ prāṇakṣayakaraḥ śoṣaṇas tu śarīriṇām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.29"> uttaro mārutaḥ snigdho mṛdurmadhura eva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               kaṣāyānurasaḥ śīto doṣāṇāṃ cāprakopaṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.20.30"> tasmāc ca prakṛtisthānāṃ kledano balavardhanaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣīṇakṣayaviṣārtānāṃ viśeṣeṇa tu pūjitaḥ || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne hitāhitīyo nāma viṃśo
                              'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>




                    <div n="21" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.1"> athāto vraṇapraśnam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.3"> vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva dehasaṃbhavahetavaḥ | tair
                              evāvyāpannair adhomadhyor dhvasanniviṣṭaiḥ śarīramidaṃ dhāryate 'gāram
                              iva sthūṇābhis tisṛbhir ataś ca tristhūṇamāhureke | ta eva ca
                              vyāpannāḥ pralayahetavaḥ | tadebhir eva śoṇitacaturthaiḥ saṃbhavasth
                              itipralayeṣv apyavirahitaṃ śarīraṃ bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.4"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               narte dehaḥ kaphād asti na pittānna ca mārutāt |
                              <caesura/>
                               śoṇitād api vā nityaṃ deha etais tu dhāryate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.5"> tatra vā gatigandhanayor iti dhātuḥ tapa santāpe
                              śliṣa āliṅgane eteṣāṃ kṛdvihitaiḥ pratyayair vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmeti ca
                              rūpāṇi bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.6"> doṣasthānānyata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra samāsena
                              vātaḥ śroṇigudasaṃśrayaḥ taduparyadho nābheḥ pakvāśayaḥ
                              pakvāmāśayamadhyaṃ pittasya āmāśayaḥ śleṣmaṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.7"> ataḥ paraṃ pañcadhā vibhajyante | tatra vātasya
                              vātavyādhau vakṣyāmaḥ pittasya yakṛtplīhānau hṛdayaṃ dṛṣtistvak
                              pūrvoktaṃ ca śleṣmaṇastūraḥśiraḥkaṇṭhasandhaya iti pūrvoktaṃ ca etāni
                              khalu doṣāṇāṃ sthānānyavyāpannānām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.8"> visargādānavikṣepaiḥ somasūryānilā yathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhārayanti jagaddehaṃ kaphapittānilās tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.9"> tatra jijñāsyaṃ kiṃ pittavyatirekādanyo 'gniḥ
                              āhosvit pittamevāgnir iti | atrocyate na khalu pittavyatirekādanyo
                              'gnirupalabhyate āgneyatvāt pitte dahanapacanādiṣvabhipravartamāneṣv
                              agnivadupacāraḥ kriyate 'ntaragnir iti kṣiṇe hy agniguṇe
                              tatsamānadravyopayogādativṛddhe śītakriyopayogādāgamāc ca paśyāmo na
                              khalu pittavyatirekādanyo 'gnir iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.10"> taccādṛṣṭahetukena viśeṣeṇa pakvāmāśayamadhyasthaṃ
                              pittaṃ caturvidhamannapānaṃ pacati vivecayati ca doṣarasamūtrapurīṣāṇi
                              tatrastham eva cātmaśaktyā śeṣāṇāṃ pittasthānānāṃ śarīrasya
                              cāgnikarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ karoti tasmin pitte pācako 'gnir iti saṃjñā yat
                              tu yakṛtplīhnoḥ pittaṃ tasmin rañjako 'gnir iti saṃjñā sa rasasya
                              rāgakṛduktaḥ yat pittaṃ hṛdayasaṃsthaṃ tasmin sādhako 'gnir iti saṃjñā
                              so 'bhiprārthitamanorathasādhanakṛduktaḥ yaddṛṣṭyāṃ pittaṃ
                              tasminnālocako 'gnir iti saṃjñā sa rūpagrahaṇādhikṛtaḥ yat tu tvaci
                              pittaṃ tasmin bhrājako 'gnir iti saṃjñā so
                              'bhyaṅgapariṣekāvagāhāvalepanādīnāṃ kriyādravyāṇāṃ paktā chāyānāṃ ca
                              prakāśakaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.11"> pittaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ dravam pūti nīlaṃ pītaṃ tathaiva ca
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               uṣṇaṃ kaṭurasaṃ caiva vidagdhaṃ cāmlam eva ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.12"> ata ūrdhvaṃ śleṣmasthānānyanuvyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra
                              āmāśayaḥ pittāśayasyopariṣṭhāttatpratyanīkatvād ūrdhvagatitvāt tejasaś
                              candra iva ādityasya sa caturvidhasyāhārasyādhāraḥ sa ca tatraudakair
                              guṇair āhāraḥ praklinno bhinnasaṃghātaḥ sukhajaraś ca bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.13"> mādhuryāt picchilatvāc ca prakleditvāt tathaiva ca
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               āmāśaye saṃbhavati śleṣmā madhuraśītalaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.14"> sa tatrastha eva svaśaktyā śeṣāṇāṃ śleṣmasthānānāṃ
                              śarīrasya codakakarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ karoti
                              uraḥsthastrikasandhāraṇamātmavīryeṇānnarasasahitena hṛdayāvalambanaṃ
                              karoti jihvāmūlakaṇṭhastho jihvendriyasya saumyatvāt samyagrasajñāne
                              vartate śiḥrasthaḥ snehasaṃtarpaṇādhikṛtatvād
                              indriyāṇāmātmavīryeṇānugrahaṃ karoti sandhisthas tu śleṣmā
                              sarvasandhisaṃśleṣāt sarvasandhyagranuhaṃ karoti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.15"> śleṣmā śveto guruḥ snigdhaḥ picchilaḥ śīta eva ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               madhurastvavigdhaḥ syādvidagdho lavaṇaḥ srṃtaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.16"> śoṇitasya sthānaṃ yakṛtplīhānau tac ca
                              prāgabhihitaṃ tatrastham eva śeṣāṇāṃ śoṇitasthānānāmanugrahaṃ karoti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.17"> anuṣṇaśītaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ raktaṃ ca varṇataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               śoṇitaṃ guru visraṃ syādvidāhaś cāsya pittavat || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.18"> etāni khalu doṣasthānāni eṣu saṃcīyante doṣāḥ |
                              prāk saṃcayahetur uktaḥ | tatra saṃcitānāṃ khalu doṣāṇāṃ
                              stabdhapūrṇakoṣṭhatā pītāvabhāsatā mandoṣmatā cāṅgānāṃ gauravamālasyaṃ
                              cayakāraṇavidveṣaś ceti liṅgāni bhavanti | tatra prathamaḥ kriyākālaḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.19"> ata ūrdhvaṃ prakopaṇāni vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra
                              balavadvigrahātivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanaprapatanapradhāvanaprapīḍanābhighātalaṅghanaplavanataraṇarātrijāgaraṇabhāraharaṇagajaturagarathapadāticaryākaṭukaṣāyatiktarūkṣalaghuśītavīryaśuṣkaśākavallūravarakoddālakakoradūṣaśyāmākanīvāramudgamasūrāḍhakīhareṇukalāyaniṣpāvānaśanaviṣamāśanādhyaśanavātamūtrapurīṣaśukracchardikṣavathūdgārabāṣpavegavighātādibhir
                              viśeṣair vāyuḥ prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.20"> sa śītābhrapravāteṣu gharmānte ca viśeṣataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pratyūṣasyaparāhṇe tu jīrṇe 'nne ca prakupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.21">
                              krodhaśokabhayāyāsopavāsavidagdhamaithunopagamanakaṭvamlalavaṇatīkṣṇoṣṇalaghuvidāhitilatailapiṇyākakulatthasarṣapātasīharitakaśākagodhāmatsyājāvikamāṃsadadhitakrakūrcikāmastusauvīrakasurāvikārāmlaphalakaṭvaraprabhṛtibhiḥ
                              pittaṃ prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.22"> taduṣṇair uṣṇakāle ca meghānte ca viṣeśataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               madhyāhne cārdharātre ca jīryatyanne ca kupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.23">
                              divāsvapnāvyāyāmālasyamadhurāmlalavaṇaśītasnigdhagurupicchilābhiṣyandihāyanakayavakanaiṣadhetkaṭamāṣamahāmāṣagodhūma-tila-piṣṭa-vikṛtidadhidugdhakṛśarāpāyasekṣu-vikārānūpaudakamāṃsavasābisamṛṇālakaserukaśṛṅgāṭakamadhura-vallī-phalasamaśanādhyaśanaprabhṛtibhiḥ
                              śleṣmā prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.24"> sa śītaiḥ śītakāle ca vasante ca viśeṣataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pūrvāhṇe ca pradoṣe ca bhuktamātre prakupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.25"> pittaprakopaṇair eva cābhīkṣṇaṃ
                              dravasnigdhagurubhir āhārair
                              divāsvapnakrodhānalātapaśramābhighātājīrṇaviruddhādhyaśanādibhir
                              viśeṣair asṛk prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.26"> yasmādraktmaṃ vinā doṣair nā kadācit prakupyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmāt tasya yathādoṣaṃ kālaṃ vidyātprakopaṇe || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.27"> teṣāṃ prakopāt
                              koṣṭhatodasaṃcaraṇāmlikāpipāsāparidāhānnadveṣahṛdayotkledāś ca jāyante
                              | tatra dvitīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.28"> ata ūrdhvaṃ prasaraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ teṣām ebhir
                              ātaṅkaviśeṣaiḥ prakupitānāṃ (paryuṣita) kiṇvodakapiṣṭasamavāya
                              ivodriktānāṃ prasaro bhavati | teṣāṃ vāyur gatimattvāt prasaraṇahetuḥ
                              saty apy acaitanye | sa hi rajobhūyiṣṭhaḥ rajaś ca pravartakaṃ
                              sarvabhāvānām | yathā mahānudakasaṃcayo 'tivṛddhaḥ
                              setumavadāryāpareṇodakena vyāmiśraḥ sarvataḥ pradhāvati evaṃ doṣāḥ
                              kadācidekaśo dviśaḥ samastāḥ śoṇitasahitā vā'nekadhā prasaranti | tad
                              yathā vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmā śoṇitaṃ vātapitte vātaśleṣmāṇau
                              pittaśleṣmāṇau vātaśoṇite pittaśoṇite śleṣmaśoṇite vātapittaśoṇitāni
                              vātaśleṣmaśoṇitāni pittaśleṣmaśoṇitāni vātapittakaphāḥ
                              vātapittakaphaśoṇitāni ity evaṃ pañcadaśadhā prasanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.29"> kṛtsne 'rdhe 'vayave vā'pi yatrāṅge kupito bhṛśam |
                              <caesura/>
                               doṣo vikāraṃ nabhasi meghavattatra varṣati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.30"> nātyarthaṃ kupitaś cāpi līno mārgeṣu tiṣṭhati |
                              <caesura/>
                               niṣpratyanīkaḥ kālena hetumāsādya kupyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.31"> tatra vāyoḥ pittasthānagatasya pittavat pratīkāraḥ
                              pittasya ca kaphasthānagatasya kaphavat kaphasya ca vātasthānagatasya
                              vātavat eṣa kriyāvibhāgaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.32"> evaṃ prakupitānāṃ prasaratāṃ ca vāyor
                              vimārgagamanāṭopau oṣacoṣaparidāhadhūmāyanāni pittasya
                              arocakāvipākāṅgasādāś chardiś ceti śleṣmaṇo liṅgāni bavanti tatra
                              tṛtīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.33"> ata ūrdhvaṃ sthānasaṃśrayaṃ | evaṃ prakupitāḥ
                              tāṃstān śarīrapradeśānāgamya tāṃstān vyādhīn janayanti | te
                              yadodarasanniveśaṃ kurvanti tadā
                              gulmavidradhyudarāgnisaṅgānāhavisūcikātisāraprabhṛtīn janayanti
                              bastigatāḥ pramehāśmarīmūtrāghātamūtradoṣaprabhṛtīn vṛṣaṇagatā vṛddhīḥ
                              meḍhragatā niruddhaprakaśopadaṃśaśūkadoṣaprabhṛtīn gudagatā
                              bhagandarārśaḥprabhṛtīn ūrdhvajatrugatāstūrdhvajān
                              tavaṅnāṃsaśoṇitasthāḥ kṣudrarogān kuṣṭhāni visarpāṃś ca medogatā
                              granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍālajīprabhṛtīn asthigatā
                              vidradhyanuśayīprabhṛtīn pādagatāḥ
                              ślīpadavātaśoṇitavātakaṇṭakaprabhṛtīn sarvāṅgāgatā
                              jvarasaravāṅgarogaprabhṛtīn teṣāmevamabhiniviṣṭānāṃ
                              pūrvarūpaprādurbhāvaḥ taṃ pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra pūrvarūpagateṣu
                              caturthaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.34"> ata ūrdhvaṃ vyādherdarśanaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
                              śophārbudagranthividradhivisarpaprabhṛtīnāṃ pravyaktalakṣaṇatā
                              jvarātīsāraprabhṛtīnāṃ ca | tatra pañcamaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.35"> ata ūrdhvameteṣāmavadīrṇānāṃ braṇabhāvamāpannānāṃ
                              ṣaṣṭhaḥ kriyākālaḥ jvarātisāraprabhṛtīnāṃ ca dīrghakālānubandhaḥ |
                              tatrāpratikriyamāṇe 'sādhyatām upayānti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.36"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃcayaṃ ca prakopaṃ ca prasaraṃ sthānasaṃśrayam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vyaktiṃ bhedaṃ ca yo vetti doṣāṇāṃ sa bhavedbhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.37"> saṃcaye 'pahṛtā doṣā labhante nottarā gatīḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               te tūttarāsu gatiṣu bhavanti balavattarāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.38"> sarvair bhāvais tribhir vā'pi dvābhyāmekena vā
                              punaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃsarge kupitaḥ kruddhaṃ doṣaṃ doṣo 'nudhāvati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.39"> saṃsarge yo garīyān syādupakramyaḥ sa vai bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               śeṣadoṣāvirodhena sannipāte tathaiva ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.21.40"> vṛṇoti yasmāt rūḍhe 'pi vraṇavas tu na naśyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               ādehadhāraṇāttasmād draṇa ity ucyate budhaiḥ || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrashtāne vraṇapraśnādhyāyo
                              nāmaikaviṃśodhyāyaḥ </p>
                    </div>



                    <div n="22" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.1"> athāto vraṇāsrāvavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyamaḥ
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.3"> tvaṅnāṃsasirāsnāyvasthisandhikoṣṭhamarmāṇītyaṣṭau
                              vraṇavastūni | atra sarvavraṇasanniveśaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.4"> tatra ādyaikavastusanniveśī tvagbhedī vraṇaḥ
                              sūpacaraḥ śeṣāḥ svayamavaddīryamāṇā durupacārāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.5"> tatrāyataś caturasro vṛttastripuṭaka iti
                              vraṇākṛtisamāsaḥ śeṣās tu vikṛtākṛtayo durupakramā bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.6"> sarva eva vraṇāḥ kṣipraṃ saṃrohantyātmavatāṃ
                              subhiṣagbhiś copakrāntāḥ anātmavatāmajñaiś copakrāntāḥ praduṣyanti
                              pravṛddhatvāc ca doṣāṇāṃ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.7"> tatrātisaṃvṛto 'tivivṛto 'tikaṭhino 'timṛdurutsanno
                              'vasanno 'tiśīto 'tyuṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaraktapītaśuklādīnāṃ varṇānām
                              anyatamavarṇo bhairavaḥ pūtipūyamāṃsasirāsnāyuprabhṛtibhiḥ pūrṇaḥ
                              pūtipūyāsrāvyunmārgyutsaṅgyamanojñadarśanagandho 'tyarthaṃ vedanāvān
                              dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūśophapiḍakopadruto 'tyarthaṃ duṣṭaśoṇitāsrāvī
                              dīrghakālānubandhī ceti duṣṭavraṇaliṅgāni | tasya doṣocchrāyeṇa
                              ṣaṭtvaṃ vibhajya yathāsvaṃ pratīkāre prayateta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.8a"> ata ūrdhvaṃ sarvasrāvān vakṣyāmaḥ tatra ghṛṣṭāsu
                              chinnāsu vā tvakṣu sphoṭeṣu bhinneṣu vidāriteṣu vā salilaprakāśo
                              bhavatyāsrāvaḥ kiṃcidvisraḥ pītāvabhāsaś ca māṃsagataḥ sadyaś chinnāsu
                              sirāsu raktātipravṛttiḥ pakvāsu ca toyanāḍībhir iva toyāgamanaṃ
                              pūyasya āsrāvaś cātra tanur vicchinnaḥ picchilo 'valambī śyāvo
                              'vaśyāyapratimaś ca snāyugataḥ snigdho ghanaḥ siṃghāṇakapratimaḥ
                              saraktaś ca asthigato 'sthanyabhihate sphuṭite bhinne doṣāvadārite vā
                              doṣabhakṣitatvād asthi niḥsāraṃ śuktidhautamivābhāti āsrāvaś cātra
                              majjamiśraḥ sarudhiraḥ snigdhaś ca saṃdhigataḥ pīḍyamāno na pravartate
                              ākuñcanaprasāraṇonnamanavinamanapradhāvanotkāsanapravāhaṇaiś ca
                              sravati āsrāvaś cātra picchilo 'valambī saphenapūyarudhironmathitaś ca
                              koṣṭhagato 'sṛṅnūtrapurīṣapūyodakāni sravati marmagatas tvagādiṣv
                              avaruddhatvān nocyate | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.8b">tatra tvagādigatānāmāsrāvāṇāṃ yathākramaṃ
                              pāruṣyaśyāvāvaśyāyadadhimastukṣārodakamāṃsadhāvanapulākodakasannibhatvāni
                              mārutādbhavanti pittād
                              gomedagomūtrabhasmaśaṅkhakaṣāyodakamādhvīkatailasannibhatvāni
                              pittavadraktādativisratvaṃ ca
                              kaphānnavanītakāsīsamajjapiṣṭatilanārikelodakavarāhavasāsannibhatvāni
                              sannipātānnārikelodakair
                              vārukarasakāñjikaprasādārukodakapriyaṅguphalayakṛnmudgayūṣasavarṇatvānīti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.9"> ślokau cātra bhavataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pakvāśayādasādhyas tu pulākodakasannibhiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣārodakanibhaḥ srāvo varjyo raktāśayātsravan || </l>



                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.10"> āmāśayāt kalāyāmbhonibhaś ca trikasandhijaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               srāvānetān parīkṣyādau tataḥ karmācared bhiṣak ||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.11"> ata ūrdhvaṃ sarvavraṇavedanā vakṣyāmaḥ
                              todanabhedanatāḍanacchedanāyamanamanthanavikṣepaṇacum
                              cumāyananirdahanāvabhañjanasphoṭanavidāraṇotpāṭanakampanavividhaśūlaviśleṣaṇavikiraṇapūraṇastambhanasvapnākuñcanāṅkuśikāḥ
                              saṃbhavanti animittavividhavedanāprādurbhāvo vā muhurmuhur
                              yatrāgacchanti vedanāviśeṣāstaṃ vātikam iti vidyāt
                              oṣacoṣaparidāhadhūmāyanāni yatra gātramaṅgārāvakīrṇam iva pacyate
                              yatra coṣmābhivṛddhiḥ kṣate kṣārāvasiktavac ca vedanāviśeṣāstaṃ
                              paittikam iti vidyāt pittavadraktasamutthaṃ jānīyāt kaṇḍūrgurutvaṃ
                              suptatvam upadeho 'lpavedanatvaṃ stambhaḥ śaityaṃ ca yatra taṃ
                              ślaiṣmikam iti vidyāt yatra sarvāsāṃ vedanānām utpattis taṃ
                              sānnipātikam iti vidyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.12"> ata ūrdhvaṃ vraṇavarṇān vakṣyāmaḥ
                              bhasmakapotāsthivarṇaḥ paruṣo 'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇa iti mārutajasya nīlaḥ pīto
                              haritaḥ śyāvaḥ kṛṣṇo raktaḥ kapilaḥ piṅgala iti raktapittasamutthayoḥ
                              śvetaḥ snigdhaḥ pāṇḍur iti śleṣmajasya sarvavarṇopetaḥ sānnipātika iti
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.22.13"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               na kevalaṃ vraṇeṣūkto vedanāvarṇasaṃgrahaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sarvaśophavikāreṣu vraṇaval lakṣayed bhiṣak || </l>
                    </div>




                    <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.1"> athātaḥ kṛtyākṛtyavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.3"> tatra vayaḥsthānāṃ dṛḍhānāṃ prāṇavatāṃ sattvavatāṃ
                              ca sucikitsyā vraṇāḥekasmin vā puruṣe yatraitad guṇacatuṣṭayaṃ tasya
                              sukhasādhanīyatamāḥ | tatra vayaḥsthānāṃ pratyagradhātutvād āśu vraṇā
                              rohanti dṛḍhānāṃ sthirabahumāṃsatvāc chastram avacāryamāṇaṃ
                              sirāsnāyvādiviśeṣān na prāpnoti prāṇavatāṃ
                              vedanābhighātāhārayantraṇādibhir na glānir utpadyate sattvavatāṃ
                              dāruṇair api kriyāviśeṣair na vyathā bhavati tasmād eteṣāṃ
                              sukhasādhanīyatamāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.4"> ta eva viparītaguṇā vṛddhakṛśālpaprāṇabhīruṣu
                              draṣṭavyāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.5">
                              sphikpāyuprajananalalāṭagaṇḍauṣṭhapṛṣṭhakarṇaphalakoṣodarajatrumukhābhyantarasaṃsthāḥ
                              sukharopaṇīyā vraṇāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.6">
                              akṣidantanāsāpāṅgaśrotranābhijaṭharasevanīnitambapārśvakukṣivakṣaḥkakṣāstanasandhibhāgagatāḥ
                              saphenapūyaraktānilavāhino 'ntaḥśalyāś ca duścikitsyāḥ adhobhāgāś
                              cordhvabhāganirvāhiṇo romāntopanakhamarmajaṅghāsthisaṃśritāś ca
                              bhagandaram api cāntarmukhaṃ sevanīkuṭakāsthisaṃśritam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.7"> kuṣṭhināṃ viṣajuṣṭānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ madhumehinām |
                              <caesura/>
                               vraṇāḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyanti yeṣāṃ cāpi vraṇe vraṇāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.8">
                              avapāṭikāniruddhaprakaśasanniruddhagudajaṭharagranthikṣatakrimayaḥ
                              pratiśyāyajāḥ koṣṭhajāś ca tvagdoṣiṇāṃ pramehiṇāṃ vā ye parikṣateṣu
                              dṛśyante śarkarā sikatāmeho vātakuṇḍalikā'ṣṭhīlā dantaśarkaropakuśaḥ
                              kaṇṭhaśālūkaṃ niṣkoṣaṇadūṣitāś ca dantaveṣṭā
                              visarpāsthikṣatoraḥkṣatavraṇagranthiprabhṛtayaś ca yāpyāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.9"> sādhyā yāpyatvam āyānti yāpyāś cāsādhyatāṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               ghnanti prāṇān asādhyās tu narāṇām akriyāvatām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.10"> yāpanīyaṃ vijānīyāt kriyā dhārayate tu yam |
                              <caesura/>
                               kriyāyāṃ tu nivṛttāyāṃ sadya eva vinaśyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.11"> prāptā kriyā dhārayati yāpyavayādhitam āturam |
                              <caesura/>
                               prapatiṣyadivāgāraṃ viṣkambhaḥ sādhuyojitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.12"> ata ūrdhvam asādhyān vakṣyāmaḥ māṃsapiṇḍavad
                              udgatāḥ prasekino 'ntaḥpūyavedanāvanto 'śvāpānavad udvṛttauṣṭhāḥ kecit
                              kaṭhinā gośṛṅgavad unnatamṛdumāṃsaprarohāḥ apare
                              duṣṭarudhirāsrāviṇastanuśītapicchilasrāviṇo vā madhyonnatāḥ kecid
                              avasannaśuṣiraparyantāḥ śaṇatūlavat snāyujālavanto durdarśanāḥ
                              vasāmedomajjamastuluṅgasrāviṇaś ca doṣasamutthāḥ
                              pītāsitamūtrapurīṣavātavāhinaś ca koṣṭhasthāḥ ta
                              evobhayatobhāgavraṇamukheṣu pūyaraktanirvāhiṇaḥ (ā.kṣīṇamāṃsānāṃ ca)
                              sarvato gatayaś cāṇumukhā māṃsabudbudavantaḥ saśabdavātavāhinaś ca
                              śiraḥkaṇṭhasthāḥ kṣīṇamāṃsānāṃ ca pūyaraktanirvāhiṇo
                              'rocakāvipākakāsaśvāsopadravayuktāḥ bhinne vā śiraḥkapāle yatra
                              mastuluṅgadarśanaṃ tridoṣaliṅgaprādurbhāvaḥ kāsaśvāsau vā yasyeti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.13"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               vasāṃ medo 'tha majjānaṃ mastuluṅgaṃ ca yaḥ sravet |
                              <caesura/>
                               āgantus tu vraṇaḥ sidhyen na sidhyed doṣasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.14"> amarmopahite deśe sirāsandhyasthivarjite |
                              <caesura/>
                               vikāro yo 'nuparyeti tad asādhyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.15"> krameṇopacayaṃ prāpya dhatūn anugataḥ śanaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               na śakya unmūlayituṃ vṛddho vṛkṣa ivāmayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.16"> sa sthiratvān mahattvāc ca dhātvanukramaṇena ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               nihantyauṣadhavīryāṇi mantrān duṣṭagraho yathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.17"> ato yo viparītaḥ syāt sukhasādhyaḥ sa ucyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               abaddhamūlaḥ kṣupako yadvad utpāṭane sukhaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.18"> tribhir doṣair anākrāntaḥ śyāvauṣṭhaḥ piḍakī samaḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               avedano nirāsrāvo vraṇaḥ śuddha ihocyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.19"> kapotavarṇapratimā yasyāntāḥ kledavarjitāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sthirāś cipiṭikāvanto rohatīti tam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.20"> rūḍhavartmānam agranthim aśūnam arujaṃ vraṇam |
                              <caesura/>
                               tvaksavarṇaṃ samatalaṃ samyag rūḍhaṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.23.21"> doṣaprakopād vyāyāmādabhighātādajīrṇataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               harṣāt krodhād bhayād vā 'pi vraṇo rūḍho 'pi dīryate || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne kṛtyākṛtyavidhirnāma
                              trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>

                    <div n="24" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.1"> athāto vyādhisamuddeśīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.3"> dvividhās tu vyādhayaḥ śastrasādhyāḥ
                              snehādikriyāsādhyāś ca | tatra śastrasādhyeṣu snehādikriyā na
                              pratiṣidhyate snehādikriyāsādhyeṣu śastrakarma na kriyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.4"> asmin punaḥ śāstre sarvatantrasāmānyāt sarveṣāṃ
                              vyādhīnāṃ yathāsthūlam avarodhaḥ kriyate | prāgabhihitaṃ
                              tadduḥkhasaṃyogā vyādhaya iti | tac ca duḥkhaṃ trividhaṃ ādhyātmikaṃ
                              ādhibhautikaṃ ādhidaivikam iti | tat tu saptavidhe vyādhāv upanipatati
                              | te punaḥ saptavidhā vyādhayaḥ tad yathā ādibalapravṛttāḥ
                              janmabalapravṛttāḥ doṣabalapravṛttāḥ saṃghātabalapravṛttāḥ
                              kālabalapravṛttāḥ daivabalapravṛttāḥ svabhāvabalapravṛttā iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.5"> tatrādibalapravṛttā ye śukraśoṇitadoṣānvayāḥ
                              kuṣṭhārśaḥprabhṛtayaḥ te 'pi dvividhāḥ mātṛjāḥ pitṛjāś ca |
                              janmabalapravṛttā ye māturapacārāt
                              paṅgujātyandhabadhiramūkaminminavāmanaprabhṛtayo jāyante te 'pi
                              dvividhā rasakṛtāḥ dauhṛdāpacārakṛtāś ca | doṣabalapravṛttā ya
                              ātaṅkasamutpannā mithyāhārācārakṛtāś ca te 'pi dvividhāḥ
                              āmāśayasamutthāḥ pakvāśayasamutthāś ca | punaś ca dvividhāḥ śārīrā
                              mānasāś ca | ta ete ādhyātmikāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.6"> saṃghātabalapravṛttā ya āgantavo durbalasya
                              balavadvigrahāt te 'pi dvividhāḥ śastrakṛtā vyālakṛtāś ca | ete
                              ādhibhautikāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.7a"> kālabalapravṛttā ye
                              śītoṣṇavātavarṣāprabhṛtinimittāḥ te 'pi dvividhāḥ vyāpannartukṛtā
                              avyāpannartukṛtāś ca |</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.7"> daivabalapravṛttā ye devadrohādabhiśastakā
                              atharvaṇakṛtā upasargajāś ca te 'pi dvividhāḥ vidyudaśanikrtāḥ
                              piśācādikṛtāś ca punaś ca dvividhāḥ saṃsargajā ākasmikāś ca |
                              svabhāvabalapravṛttāḥ kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprabhṛtayaḥ te 'pi
                              dvividhāḥ kālakṛtā akālakṛtāś ca tatra parirakṣaṇakṛtāḥ kālakṛtāḥ
                              aparirakṣaṇakṛtā akālakṛtāḥ | ete ādhidaivikāḥ | atra
                              sarvavyādhyavarodhaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.8"> sarveṣāṃ ca vyādhīnāṃ vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva mūlaṃ
                              talliṅgatvād dṛṣṭaphalatvād āgamāc ca | yathā hi kṛtsnaṃ vikārajātaṃ
                              viśvarūpeṇāvasthitaṃ sattva<pc> </pc>rajas<pc> </pc>tamāṃsi na
                              vyatiricyante evam eva kṛtsnaṃ vikārajātaṃ viśvarūpeṇāvasthitam
                              avyatiricya vātapittaśleṣmāṇo vartante | doṣadhātumalasaṃsargād
                              āyatanaviśeṣān nimittataś caiṣāṃ vikalpaḥ | doṣadūṣiteṣv atyarthaṃ
                              dhātuṣu saṃjñā kriyate rasajo 'yaṃ śoṇitajo 'yaṃ māṃsajo 'yaṃ medojo
                              'yaṃ asthijo 'yaṃ majjajo 'yaṃ śukrajo 'yam vyādhir iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.9"> tatra
                              annāśraddhārocakāvipākāṅgamardajvarahṛllāsatṛptigauravahṛtpāṇḍurogamārgoparodhakārśyavairasyāṅgasādākālavalipalitadarśanaprabhṛtayo
                              rasadoṣajā vikārāḥ
                              kuṣṭhavisarpapiḍakāmaśakanīlikātilakālakanyacchavyaṅgendraluptaplīhavidradhigulmavātaśoṇitārśo
                              'rbudāṅgamardāsṛgdararaktapittaprabhṛtayo raktadoṣajāḥ
                              gudamukhameḍhrapākāś ca adhimāṃsārbudārśo
                              'dhijihvopajihvopakuśagalaśuṇḍikālajīmāṃsasaṃghātauṣṭhaprakopagalagaṇḍagaṇḍamālāprabhṛtayo
                              māṃsadoṣajāḥ
                              granthivṛddhigalagaṇḍārbudamedojauṣṭhaprakopamadhumehātisthaulyātisvedaprabhṛtayo
                              medodoṣajāḥ adhyasthyadhidantāsthitodaśūlakunakhaprabhṭayo
                              'sthidoṣajāḥ
                              tamodarśanamūrcchābhramaparvasthūlamūlārurjanmanetrābhisyandaprabhṛtayo
                              majjadoṣajāḥ klaibyāpraharṣaśukrāśmarīśukramehaśukradoṣādayaś ca
                              taddoṣajāḥ tvagdoṣāḥ saṅgo 'tipravṛttirayathāpravṛttir vā
                              malāyatanadoṣāḥ indriyāṇām apravṛttir ayathā pravṛttir
                              vendriyāyatanadoṣāḥ ity eṣa samāsa uktaḥ vistaraṃ nimittāni caiṣāṃ
                              pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.10"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               kupitānāṃ hi doṣāṇāṃ śarīre paridhāvatām |
                              <caesura/>
                               yatra saṅgaḥ khavaiguṇyād vyādhis tatropajāyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.11"> bhūyo 'tra jijñāsyaṃ kiṃ vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ ca
                              nityaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ paricchedo vā iti yadi nityaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ syāt tarhi
                              nityāturāḥ sarva eva prāṇinaḥ syuḥ athāpy anyathā vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ
                              cānyatra vartamānānām anyatra liṅgaṃ na bhavatīti kṛtvā yad ucyate
                              vātādayo jvarādīnāṃ mūlānīti tan na | atrocyate doṣān pratyākhyāya
                              jvarādayo na bhavanti atha ca na nityaḥ saṃbandhaḥ yathā hi
                              vidyudvātāśanivarṣāṇyākāśaṃ pratyākhyāya na bhavanti saty apy ākāśe
                              kadācin na bhavanti atha ca nimittatas tata evotpattir iti
                              taraṅgabudbudādayaś codakaviśeṣāḥ eva vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ ca nāpy
                              evam saṃśleṣo na paricchedaḥ śāśvatikaḥ atha ca nimittata evotpattir
                              iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.24.12"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               vikāraparimāṇaṃ ca saṃkhyā caiṣāṃ pṛthak pṛthak |
                              <caesura/>
                               vistareṇottare tantre sarvā bādhāś ca vakṣyate || </l>


                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vyādhisamuddeśīyo nāma
                              caturviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="25" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>pañcaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.1"> athāto 'ṣṭavidhaśastrakarmīyam adhyāyaṃ
                              vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.3"> chedyā bhagandarā granthiḥ ślaiṣmikastilakālakaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               vraṇavartmārbudānyarśaś carmakīlo 'sthimāṃsagam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.4"> śalyaṃ jatumaṇirmāṃsasaṃghāto galaśuṇḍikā |
                              <caesura/>
                               srāyumāṃsasirākotho valmīkaṃ śataponakaḥ || </l>


                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.5"> adhruṣaś copadaṃśāś ca māṃsakandyadhimāṃsakaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhedyā vidradhayo 'nyatra sarvajād granthayastrayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.6"> ādito ye visarpāś ca vṛddhayaḥ savidārikāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pramehapiḍakāśophastanarogāvamanthakāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.7"> kumbhīkānuśayīnāḍyo vṛndau puṣkarikālajī |
                              <caesura/>
                               prāyaśaḥ kṣudrarogāś ca puppuṭau tāludantajau || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.8"> tuṇḍikerī gilāyuś ca pūrvaṃ ye ca prapākiṇaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               bastis tathā'śmarīhetormedojā ye ca kecana || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.5-8"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.9"> lekhyāś catasro rohiṇyaḥ kilāsam upajihvikā |
                              <caesura/>
                               medojo dantavaidarbho granthir vartmādhijihvikā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.10ab"> arśāṃsi maṇḍalaṃ māṃsakandī māṃsonnatis tathā | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.10cd"> vedhyāḥ sirā bahuvidhā mūtravṛddhirdakodaram || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.11-12ab"> eṣyā nāḍyaḥ saśalyāś ca vraṇā unmārgiṇaś ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               āhāryāḥ śarkarās tisro dantakarṇamalo 'śmarī ||
                              <caesura/>
                               śalyāni mūḍhagarbhāś ca varcaś ca nicitaṃ gude | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.12cd"> srāvyā vidradhayaḥ pañca bhaveyuḥ sarvajādṛte || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.13"> kuṣṭhāni vāyuḥ sarujaḥ śopho yaś caikadeśajaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pālyāmayāḥ ślīpadāni viṣajuṣṭaṃ ca śoṇitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.14"> arbudāni visarpāś ca granthayaś cāditas tu ye |
                              <caesura/>
                               trayas trayaś copadaṃśāḥ stanarogā vidārikā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.15"> suṣiro galaśālūkaṃ kaṇṭakāḥ kṛmidantakaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dantaveṣṭaḥ sopakuśaḥ śītādo dantapuppuṭaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.16"> pittāsṛkkaphajāś cauṣṭhyāḥ kṣudrarogāś ca bhūyaśaḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               sīvyā medaḥsamutthāś ca bhinnāḥ sulikhitā gadāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.17"> sadyovraṇāś ca ye caiva calasandhivyapāśritāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               na kṣārāgniviṣair juṣṭā na ca mārutavāhinaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.18"> nāntarlohitaśalyāś ca teṣu samyagviśodhanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               pāṃśuromanakhādīni calamasthi bhavec ca yat || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.19"> ahṛtāni yato 'mūni pācayeyurbhṛśaṃ vraṇam |
                              <caesura/>
                               rujaś ca vividhāḥ kuryus tasmād etān viśodhayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.20"> tato vraṇaṃ samunnamya sthāpayitvā yathāsthitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               sīvyet sūkṣmeṇa sūtreṇa valkenāśmantakasya vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.21"> śaṇajakṣaumasūtrābhyāṃ snāyvā bālena vā punaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               mūrvāguḍūcītānair vā sīvyed vellitakaṃ śanaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.22"> sīvyed gophaṇikāṃ vā'pi sīvyed vā tunnasevanīm |
                              <caesura/>
                               ṛjugranthim atho vā'pi yathāyogam athāpi vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.23"> deśe 'lpamāṃse sandhau ca sūcī vṛttāṅguladvayam |
                              <caesura/>
                               āyatā tryaṅgulā tryasrā māṃsale vā'pi pūjitā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.24"> dhanurvakrā hitā marmaphalakośodaropari |
                              <caesura/>
                               ity etās trividhāḥ sūcīs tīkṣṇāgrāḥ susamāhitāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.25"> kārayen mālatīpuṣpavṛntāgraparimaṇḍalāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               nātidūre nikṛṣṭe vā sūcīṃ karmaṇi pātayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.26"> dūrādrujo vraṇauṣṭhasya sannikṛṣṭe 'valuñcanam
                              ||</l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.27"> atha kṣaumapicucchannaṃ susyūtaṃ pratisārayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               priyaṅgvañjanayaṣṭyāhvarodhracūrnaiḥ samantataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.28"> śallakīphalacūrnṇair vā kṣaumadhyāmena vā punaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               tato vraṇaṃ yathāyogaṃ baddhvācārikam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.29"> etad aṣṭavidhaṃ karma samāsena prakīrtitam |
                              <caesura/>
                               cikitsiteṣu kārtsnyena vistaras tasya vakṣyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.30"> hīnātiriktaṃ tiryak ca gātracchedanam ātmanaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               etāś catasro 'ṣṭavidhe karmaṇi vyāpadaḥ smṛtāḥ | </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.31"> ajñānalobhāhitavākyayoga
                              <caesura/>
                               bhayapramohair aparaiś ca bhāvaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               yadā prayuñjīta bhiṣak kuśastraṃ
                              <caesura/>
                               tadā sa śeṣān kurute vikārān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.32"> taṃ kṣāraśastrāgnibhir auṣadhaiś ca
                              <caesura/>
                               bhūyo 'bhiyuñjānam ayuktiyuktam |
                              <caesura/>
                               jijīviṣur dūrata eva vaidyaṃ
                              <caesura/>
                               vivarjayed ugraviṣāhitulyam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.33"> tad eva yuktaṃ tv atimarmasandhīn
                              <caesura/>
                               hiṃsyāt sirāḥ snāyum athāsthi caiva |
                              <caesura/>
                               mūrkhaprayuktaṃ puruṣaṃ kṣaṇena
                              <caesura/>
                               prāṇair viyuñjyādathavā kathaṃcit || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.34"> bhramaḥ pralāpaḥ patanaṃ pramoho
                              <caesura/>
                               viceṣṭanaṃ saṃlayanoṣṇate ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               srastāṅgatā mūrcchanam ūrdhvavāta
                              <caesura/>
                               s tīvrā rujo vātakṛtāś ca tās tāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.35"> māṃsodakābhaṃ rudhiraṃ ca gacchet
                              <caesura/>
                               sarvendriyārthoparamas tathaiva |
                              <caesura/>
                               daśārdhasaṃkhyeṣv api hi kṣateṣu sāmānyato marmasu liṅgam uktam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.36"> surendragopapratimaṃ prabhūtaṃ
                              <caesura/>
                               raktaṃ sraved vai kṣatataś ca vāyuḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               karoti rogān vividhān yathoktāṃś
                              <caesura/>
                               chinnāsu bhinnāsv athavā sirāsu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.37"> kaubjyaṃ śarīrāvayavāvasādaḥ
                              <caesura/>
                               kriyāsv aśaktis tumulā rujaś ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               cirād vraṇo rohati yasya cāpi
                              <caesura/>
                               taṃ snāyuviddhaṃ manujaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.38"> śophātivṛddhis tumulā rujaś ca
                              <caesura/>
                               balakṣayaḥ parvasu bhedaśophau |
                              <caesura/>
                               kṣateṣu sandhiṣv acalācaleṣu syāt
                              <caesura/>
                               sandhikarmoparatiś ca liṅgam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.39"> ghorā rujo yasya niśādineṣu
                              <caesura/>
                               sarvāsv avasthāsu na śāntir asti |
                              <caesura/>
                               tṛṣṇā'ṅgasādau śvayathuś ca rukṣaḥ
                              <caesura/>
                               tam asthividdhaṃ manujaṃ vyavasyet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.40"> yathāsvam etāni vibhāvayeyur
                              <caesura/>
                               liṅgāni marmasv abhitāḍiteṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               sparśaṃ na jānāti vipāṇḍuvarṇo
                              <caesura/>
                               yo māṃsamarmaṇy abhitāḍitaḥ syāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.41"> ātmānamevātha jaghanyakārī śastreṇa yo hanti hi
                              karma kurvan |
                              <caesura/>
                               tamātmāvānātmahanaṃ kuvaidyaṃ vivarjayed āyurabhīpsamānaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.42"> tiryakpraṇihite śastre doṣāḥ purvamudāhṛtāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmāt pariharan doṣān kuruyācchastranipātanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.43"> mātaraṃ pitaraṃ putrān bāndhavānapi cāturaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               apyetānabhiśaṅketa vaidye viśvāsameti ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.44"> visṛjatyātmanā+ātmānaṃ na cainaṃ pariśaṅkate |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmāt putravadevainaṃ pālayed āturaṃ bhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.45"> dharmārthau kīrtim ity arthaṃ satāṃ grahaṇam
                              uttamam |
                              <caesura/>
                               prāpnuyāt svargavāsaṃ ca hitamārabhya karmaṇā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.25.46"> karmaṇā kaścidekena dvābhyāṃ kaścittribhis tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               vikāraḥ sādhyate kaścic caturbhir api karmabhiḥ || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne 'ṣṭavidhaśastrakarmaṇyo
                              nāma pañcaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>



                    <div n="26" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.1"> athātaḥ pranaṣṭaśalyavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ
                              vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantiriḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.3"> śala śvala āśugamane dhātuḥ tasya śalyam iti rūpam
                              || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.4"> tad dvividhaṃ śārīram āgantukaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.5"> sarvaśarīrābādhakaraṃ śalyaṃ tadihopadiśyata ity
                              ataḥ śalyaśāstram || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.6"> tatra śārīraṃ romanakhādi dhātavo 'nnamalā doṣāś ca
                              duṣṭāḥ āgantv api śārīraśalyavyatirekeṇa yāvanto bhāvā duḥkham
                              utpādayanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.7"> adhikāro hi lohaveṇuvṛkṣatṛṇaśṛṅgāsthimayeṣu tatrāpi
                              viśeṣato loheṣveva viśasanārthopapannatvāllohasya lohānām api
                              durvāratvād aṇumukhatvād dūraprayojanakaratvāc ca śara evādhikṛtaḥ |
                              sa dvividhaḥ karṇī ślakṣṇaś ca prāyeṇa
                              vividhavṛkṣapatrapuṣpaphalatulyākṛtayo vyākhyātā
                              vyālamṛgapakṣivaktrasadṛśāś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.8"> sarvaśalyānāṃ tu mahatāmaṇūnāṃ vā pañcavidho
                              gativiśeṣa ūrdhvam adho 'rvācīnas tiryag ṛjur iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.9-10"> tāni vegakṣayāt pratighātād vā tvagādiṣu
                              vraṇavastuṣv avatiṣṭhante dhamanīsroto 'sthivivarapeśīprabhṛtiṣu vā
                              śarīrapradeśeṣu ||
                              <label>1931 ed. 1.26.10</label>
                               tatra śalyalakṣaṇam ucyamānam upadhāraya | tat tu dvividhaṃ sāmānyaṃ
                              vaiśeṣikaṃ ca | śyāvaṃ piḍakācitaṃ śophavedanāvantaṃ muhurmuhuḥ
                              śoṇitāsrāviṇaṃ budbudavad unnataṃ mṛdumāṃsaṃ ca vraṇaṃ jānīyāt saśalyo
                              'yam iti | sāmānyam etal lakṣaṇam uktam | vaiśeṣikaṃ tu tvaggate
                              vivarṇaḥ śopho bhavaty āyataḥ kaṭhinaś ca māṃsagate śophābhivṛddhiḥ
                              śalyamārgānupasaṃrohaḥ pīḍanāsahiṣṇutā coṣapākau ca peśyantarasthe 'py
                              etad eva coṣaśophavarjaṃ sirāgate sirādhmānam sirāśūlaṃ sirāśophaś ca
                              snāyugate snāyujālotkṣepaṇaṃ saṃrambhaś cogrā ruk ca srotogate
                              srotasāṃ svakarmaguṇahāniḥ; dhamanīsthe saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ
                              saśabdo nirgacchaty aṅgamardaḥ pipāsā hṛllāsaś ca asthigate
                              vividhavedanāprādurbhāvaḥ śophaś ca asthivivaragate
                              'sthipūrṇatā'sthitodaḥ saṃharṣo balavāṃś ca sandhigate
                              'sthivacceṣṭoparamaś ca koṣṭhagata āṭopānāhau mūtrapurīṣāhāradarśanaṃ
                              ca vraṇamukhāt marmagate marmaviddhāvac ceṣṭate | sūkṣmagatiṣu śalyeṣv
                              etāny eva lakṣaṇāny aspaṣṭāni bhavanti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.11"> mahānty alpāni vā śuddhadehānām anulomasanniviṣṭāni
                              rohanti viśeṣataḥ kaṇṭhasrotaḥsirātvakpeśyasthivivareṣu
                              doṣaprakopavyāyāmābhighātājīrṇebhyaḥ pracalitāni punarbādhante || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.12"> tatra tvakpranaṣṭe snigdhasvinnāyāṃ
                              mṛnmāṣayavagodhūmagomayamṛditāyāṃ tvaci yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā
                              bhavati tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt styānaghṛtamṛccandanakalkair vā
                              pradigdhāyāṃ śalyoṣmaṇā+āśu visarati ghṛtam upaśuṣyati vā lepo yatra
                              tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt māṃsapranaṣṭe snehasvedādibhiḥ kriyāviśeṣair
                              aviruddair āturam upapādayet karśitasya tu śithilībhūtam anavabaddhaṃ
                              kṣubhyamāṇaṃ yatra saṃrambhaṃ vedanāṃ vā janayati tatra śalyaṃ
                              vijānīyāt koṣṭhāsthisandhipeśīvivareṣv avasthitam evam eva parīkṣeta
                              sirādhamanīsrotaḥsnāyupranaṣṭe khaṇḍacakrasaṃyukte yāne vyādhitam
                              āropyāśu viṣame 'dhvani yāyād yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra
                              śalyaṃ jānīyāt asthipranaṣṭe snehasvedopapannānyasthīni
                              bandhanapīḍanābhyāṃ bhṛśam upācared yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati
                              tatra śalyaṃ jānīyāt sandhipranaṣṭe snehasvedopapannān sandhīn
                              prasaraṇākuñcanabandhanapīḍanair bhṛśam upācaret yatra saṃrambho
                              vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt marmapranaṣṭe tv ananyabhāvān
                              marmaṇām uktaṃ parīkṣaṇaṃ bhavati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.13"> sāmānyalakṣaṇam api ca
                              hastiskandhāśvapṛṣṭhaparvatadrumārohaṇadhanurvyāyāmadrutayānaniyuddhādhvagamanalaṅghanaprataraṇaplavanavyāyāmair
                              jṛmbhodgārakāsakṣavathuṣṭhīvanahasanaprāṇāyāmair
                              vātamūtrapurīṣaśukrotsargair vā yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati
                              tatra śalyaṃ jānīyāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.14"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               yasmiṃs todādayo deśo suptatā gurutā'pi ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               ghaṭṭate bahuśo yatra srūyate tudyate 'pi ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.15"> āturaś cāpi yaṃ deśam abhīkṣṇaṃ parirakṣati |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃvāhyamāno bahuśas tatra śalyaṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.16"> alpābādham aśūnaṃ ca nīrujaṃ nirupadravam |
                              <caesura/>
                               prasannaṃ mṛduparyantaṃ nirāghaṭṭamanunnatam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.17"> eṣaṇyā sarvato dṛṣṭvā yathāmārgaṃ cikitsakaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prasārākuñcanān nūnaṃ niḥśalyam iti nirdiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.18"> asthyātmakaṃ bhajyate tu śalyamantaś ca śīryate |
                              <caesura/>
                               prāyo nirbhujyate śārṅgam āyasaṃ ceti niścayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.19"> vārkṣavaiṇavatārṇāni nirhrayante tu no yadi |
                              <caesura/>
                               pacanti raktaṃ māṃsaṃ ca kṣipram etāni dehinām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.20"> kānakaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ raitikaṃ trapusīsakam |
                              <caesura/>
                               cirasthānād vilīyante pittatejaḥpratāpanāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.21"> svabhāvaśītā mṛdavo ye cānye 'pīdṛśā matāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dravībhūtāḥ śarīre 'sminn ekatvaṃ yānti dhātubhiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.22"> viṣāṇadantakeśāsthiveṇudārūpalāni tu |
                              <caesura/>
                               śalyāni na viśīryante śarīre mṛnmayāni ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.26.23"> dvividhaṃ pañcagatimattvagādivraṇavastuṣu |
                              <caesura/>
                               viśliṣṭaṃ vetti yaḥ śalyaṃ sa rājñaḥ kartum arhati || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrtasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne pranaṣṭaśalyavijñānīyo
                              nāma ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>
                    <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.1"> athātaḥ śalyāpanayanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.3"> śalyaṃ dvividhamavabaddhamanavabaddhaṃ ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.4"> tatra samāsenānavabaddhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ pañcadaśa
                              hetūn vakṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā svabhāvaḥ pācanaṃ bhedanaṃ dāraṇaṃ pīḍanaṃ
                              pramārjanaṃ nirdhmāpanaṃ vamanaṃ virecanaṃ prakṣālanaṃ pratimarśaḥ
                              pravāhaṇaṃ ācūṣaṇaṃ ayaskānto harṣaś ceti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.5"> tatrāśrukṣavathūdgārakāsamūtrapurīṣānilaiḥ
                              svabhāvabalapravṛttair nayanādibhyaḥ patati māṃsāvagāḍhaṃ
                              śalyamavidahyamānaṃ pācayitvā prakothā(ā.pā)ttasya pūyaśoṇitavegād
                              gauravād vā patati | pakvamabhidyamānaṃ bhedayed dārayed vā |
                              bhinnamanirasyamānaṃ pīḍanīyaiḥ pīḍayet pāṇibhir vā | aṇūny
                              akṣaśalyāni pariṣecanādhmāpanair bālavastrapāṇibhiḥ pramārjayet |
                              āhāraśeṣaśleṣmahīnāṇuśalyāni śvasanotkāsanapradhamanair nirdhamet |
                              annaśalyāni vamanāṅgulipratimarśaprabhṛtibhiḥ | virecanaiḥ
                              pakvāśayagatāni | vraṇadoṣāśayagatāni prakṣālanaiḥ |
                              vātamūtrapurīṣagarbhasaṅgeṣu pravāhaṇamuktaṃ |
                              mārutodakasaviṣarudhiraduṣṭastanyeṣv ācūṣaṇam āsyena viṣāṇair vā |
                              anulomam anavabaddham akarṇam analpavraṇamukham ayaskāntena | hṛdy
                              avasthitam anekakāraṇotpannaṃ śokaśalyaṃ harṣeṇeti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.6"> sarvaśalyānāṃ tu mahatām aṇūnāṃ vā dvāv
                              evāharaṇahetū bhavataḥ pratilomo 'nulomaś ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.7-8"> tatra pratilomamarvācīnamānayet anulomaṃ parācīnam
                              ||
                              <label>1931 ed. 1.27.8</label>
                               uttuṇḍitaṃ chitvā nirghātayecchedanīyamukham || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.9"> chedanīyamukhānyapi
                              kukṣivakṣaḥkakṣāvaṃkṣaṇaparśukāntarapatitāni ca hastaśakyaṃ
                              yathāmārgeṇa hastenaivāpahartuṃ prayateta || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.10"> hastenāpahartum aśakyaṃ viśasya śastreṇa
                              yantreṇāpaharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.11"> bhavati cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               śītalena jalenainaṃ mūrcchantam avasecayet |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃrakṣedasya marmāṇi muhur āśvāsayec ca tam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.12"> tataḥ śalyam uddhṛtya nirlohitaṃ vraṇaṃ kṛtvā
                              svedārham agnighṛtaprabhṛtibhiḥ saṃsvedya vidahya pradihya
                              sarpirmadhubhyāṃ baddhvā+ācārikam upadiśet | (? sirāsnāyuvilagnaṃ
                              śalākādibhir vimocyāpanayet śvayathugrastavāraṅgaṃ samavapīḍya
                              śvayathuṃ durbalavāraṅgaṃ kuśādibhir baddhvā |) </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.13"> hṛdayamabhito vartamānaṃ śalyaṃ śītajalādibhir
                              udvejitasyāpahared yathāmārgaṃ durupaharamanyato 'pabādhyamānaṃ
                              pāṭayitvoddharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.14"> asthivivarapraviṣṭam asthividaṣṭaṃ vā'vagṛhya
                              pādābhyāṃ yantreṇāpaharet aśakyamevaṃ vā balavadbhiḥ suparigṛhītasya
                              yantreṇa grāhayitvā śalyavāraṅgaṃ pravibhujya dhanurguṇair
                              baddhaikataś cāsya pañcāṅgyām upasaṃyatasyāśvasya vaktrakavike
                              badhnīyāt athainaṃ kaśayā tāḍayed yathonnamayan śiro vegena śalyam
                              uddharati dṛḍhāṃ vā vṛkṣaśākhām avanamya tasyāṃ pūrvavad
                              baddhvoddharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.15"> adeśottuṇḍitamaṣṭhīlāśmamudgarāṇāmnyatamasya
                              prahāreṇa vicālya yathāmārgam eva yantreṇa || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.16"> (? yantreṇa ) vimṛditakarṇāni
                              karṇavantyanābādhakaradeśottuṇḍitāni purastādeva || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.17"> jātuṣe kaṇṭhāsakte kaṇṭhe nāḍīṃ praveśyāgnitaptāṃ
                              ca śalākāṃ tayā 'vagṛhya śītābhir adbhiḥ pariṣicya sthirībhūtām
                              uddharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.18-21"> ajātuṣaṃ jatumadhūcchiṣṭapraliptayā śalākayā
                              pūrvakalpenetyeke ||
                              <label>1931 ed. 1.27.19</label>
                               asthiśalyamanyadvā tiryakkaṇṭhāsaktamavekṣya keśoṇḍukaṃ
                              dṛḍhaikasūtrabaddhaṃ dravabhaktopahitaṃ pāyayed ākaṇṭhāt pūrṇakoṣṭhaṃ
                              ca vāmayet vamataś ca śalyaikadeśasaktaṃ jñātvā sūtraṃ sahasā
                              tvākṣipet mṛdunā vā dantadhāvanakūrcakenāpaharet praṇudedvā'ntaḥ |
                              kṣatakaṇṭhāya ca madhusarpiṣī leḍhuṃ prayacchettriphalācūrṇaṃ vā
                              madhuśarkarāvimiśram ||
                              <label>1931 ed. 1.27.20</label>
                               udakapūrṇodaramavākśirasamavapīḍayed dhunīyādvāmayed vā bhasmarāśau
                              vā nikhanedāmukhāt ||
                              <label>1931 ed. 1.27.21</label>
                               grāsaśalye tu kaṇṭhāsakte niḥśaṅkamanavabuddhaṃ skandhe
                              muṣṭinā'bhihanyāt snehaṃ madyaṃ pānīyaṃ vā pāyayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.22"> bāhurajjulatāpāśaiḥ kaṇṭhapīḍanādvāyuḥ prakupitaḥ
                              śleṣmāṇaṃ kopayitvā sroto niruṇaddhi lālāsrāvaṃ phenāgamanaṃ
                              saṃjñānāśaṃ cāpādayati tamabhyajya saṃsvedya śirovirecanaṃ tasmai
                              tīkṣṇaṃ dadyādrasaṃ ca vātaghnaṃ vidadhyād iti || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.23"> bhavanti cātra |
                              <caesura/>
                               śalyākṛtiviśeṣāṃś ca sthānānyāvekṣya buddhimān |
                              <caesura/>
                               tathā yantrapṛthaktvaṃ ca samyak śalyamathāharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.24"> karṇavanti tu śalyāni duḥkhāhāryāṇi yāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               ādadīta bhiṣak tasmāt tāni yuktyā samāhitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.25"> etair upāyaiḥ śalyaṃ tu naiva niryātyate yadi |
                              <caesura/>
                               matyā nipuṇayā vaidyo yantrayogaiś ca nirharet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.27.26"> śothapākau rujaś cogrāḥ kuryāc chalyam anirhṛtam |
                              <caesura/>
                               vaikalyaṃ maraṇaṃ cā'pi tasmād yatnād vinirharet || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śalyāpanayanīyo nāma
                              saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>
                    <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
                         <head>aṣṭāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.1"> athāto viparītāviparītavraṇavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ
                              vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.3"> phalāgnijalavṛṣṭīnāṃ puṣpadhūmāmbudā yathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               khyāpayanti bhaviṣyatvaṃ tathā riṣṭāni pañcatām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.4"> tāni saukṣmyāt pramādād vā tathaivāśu vyatikramāt |
                              <caesura/>
                               gṛhyante nodgatāny ajñair mumūrṣor na tv asaṃbhavāt || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.5"> dhruvaṃ tu maraṇaṃ riṣṭe brāhmaṇais tat kilāmalaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               rasāyanatapojapyatatparair vā nivāryate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.6"> nakṣatrapīḍā bahudhā yathā kālād vipacyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               tathaivāriṣṭapākaṃ ca bruvate bahavo janāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.7"> asiddhim āpnuyāl loke pratikurvan gatāyuṣaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ato 'riṣṭani yatnena lakṣayet kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.8"> gandhavarṇarasādīnāṃ viśeṣāṇāṃ svabhāvataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               vaikṛtaṃ yat tad ācaṣṭe vraṇinaḥ pakvalakṣaṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.9"> kaṭus tīkṣṇaś ca visraś ca gandhas tu pavanādibhiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               lohagandhis tu raktena vyāmiśraḥ sānnipātikaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.10"> lājātasītailasamāḥ kiṃcidvisrāś ca gandhataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               jñeyāḥ prakṛtigandhāḥ syur ato 'nyad gandhavaikṛtam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.11"> madhyāgurvājyasumanaḥpadmacandanacampakaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sagandhā divyagandhāś ca mumūrṣūṇāṃ vraṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.12"> śvavājimūṣikadhvāṅkṣapūtivallūramatkuṇaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sagandhāḥ paṅkagandhāś ca bhūmigandhāś ca garhitāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.13"> dhyāmakuṅkumakaṅkuṣṭhasavarṇāḥ pittakopataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               na dahyante na cūṣyante bhiṣak tān parivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.14"> kaṇḍūmantaḥ sthirāḥ śvetāḥ snigdhāḥ kaphanimittataḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               dūyante vā'pi dahyante bhiṣak tān parivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.15"> kṛṣṇās tu ye tanusrāvā vātajā marmatāpinaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               svalpām api na kurvanti rujaṃ tān parivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.16"> kṣveḍanti ghurghurāyante jvalantīva ca ye vraṇāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               tvaṅmāṃsasthāś ca pavanaṃ saśabdaṃ visṛjanti ye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.17"> ye ca marmasvasaṃbhūtā bhavanty atyarthavedanāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               dahyante cāntaratyarthaṃ bahiḥ śītāś ca ye vraṇāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.18"> dahyante bahir atyarthaṃ bhavanty antaś ca śītalāḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               śaktidhvajarathā kuntavājivāraṇagovṛṣāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.19"> yeṣu cāpy avabhāseran prāsādākṛtayas tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               cūrṇāvakīrṇā iva ye bhānti vā na ca cūrṇitāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.20"> prāṇamāṃsakṣayaśvāsakāsārocakapīḍitāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pravṛddhapūyarudhirā vraṇā yeṣāṃ ca marmasu || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.28.21"> kriyābhiḥ samyag ārabdhā na sidhyanti ca ye vraṇāḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               varjayet tān bhiṣak prājñaḥ saṃrakṣannātmano yaśaḥ || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              viparītāviparītavraṇavijñānīyo nāmāṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
