                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.47"> keśabhasmāsthikāṣṭhāśmatuṣakārpāsakaṇṭakāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               khaṭvordhvapādā madyāpo vasā tailaṃ tilāstṛṇam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.48"> napuṃsakavyaṅgabhagnanagnamuṇḍāsitāmbarāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prasthāne vā praveśe vā neṣyante darśanaṃ gatāḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.49"> bhāṇḍānāṃ saṃkarasthānāṃ sthānāt saṃcaraṇaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               nikhātotpāṭanaṃ bhaṅgaḥ patanaṃ nirgamas tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.50"> vaidyāsanāvasādo vā rogī vā syādadhomukhaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               vaidyaṃ saṃbhāṣamāṇo 'ṅgaṃ kuḍyamā staraṇāni vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.51"> pramṛjyādvā dhunīyād vā karau pṛṣṭhaṃ śiras tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               hastaṃ cākṛṣya vaidyasya nyasec chirasi corasi || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.52"> yo vaidyamunmukhaḥ pṛcchedunmārṣṭi svāṅgamāturaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               na sa sidhyati vaidyo vā gṛhe yasya na pūjyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.52cdI"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.53"> bhavane pūjyate vā'pi yasya vaidyaḥ sa sidhyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               śubhaṃ śubheṣu dūtādiṣv aśubhaṃ hy aśubheṣu ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.54"> āturasya dhruvaṃ tasmād dūtādīn lakṣayed bhiṣak |
                              <caesura/>
                               svapnān ataḥ pravakṣyāmi maraṇāya śubhāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.55"> suhṛdo yāṃ ś ca paśyanti vyādhito vā svayaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               snehābhyaktaśarīras tu karabhavyālagardabhaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.56"> varāhair mahiṣair vā'pi yo yāyāddakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               raktāmbaradharā kṛṣṇā hasantī muktamūrdhajā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.57"> yaṃ vā karṣati baddhvā strī nṛtyantī dakṣiṇāmukham
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               antāvasāyibhir yo vā+ākṛṣyate dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.58"> pariṣvajeran yaṃ vā'pi pretāḥ pravrajitās tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               muhur āghrāyate yas tu śvāpadair vikṛtānanaiḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.59"> piben madhu ca tailaṃ ca yo vā paṅke 'vasīdati |
                              <caesura/>
                               paṅkapradigdhagātro vā pranṛtyet prahasettathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.60"> nirambaraś ca yo raktāṃ dhārayec chirasi srajam |
                              <caesura/>
                               yasya vaṃśo nalo vā'pi tālo vorasi jāyate || </l>



                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.61"> yaṃ vā matsyo grased yo vā jananīṃ praviśen naraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               parvatāgrāt pated yo vā śvabhre vā tamasā+āvṛte || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.62"> hriyate srotasā yo vā yo vā mauṇḍyam avāpnuyāt |
                              <caesura/>
                               parājīyeta badhyeta kākādyair vā'bhibhūyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.63"> patanaṃ tārakādīnāṃ praṇāśaṃ dīpacakṣuṣoḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               yaḥ paśyed devatānāṃ ca (ā.vā) prakampam avanes tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.64"> yasya chardir vireko vā daśanāḥ prapatanti vā |
                              <caesura/>
                               śālmalīṃ kiṃśukaṃ yūpaṃ valmīkaṃ pāribhadrakam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.65"> puṣpāḍhyaṃ kovidāraṃ vā citāṃ vā yo 'dhirohati |
                              <caesura/>
                               kārpāsatailapiṇyākalohāni lavaṇaṃ tilān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.66"> labhetāśnīta vā pakvam annaṃ yaś ca pibet surām |
                              <caesura/>
                               svasthaḥ sa labhate vyādhiṃ vyādhito mṛtyum ṛcchati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.67"> yathāsvaṃ prakṛtisvapno vismṛto vihatas tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               cintākṛto divā dṛṣto bhavanty aphaladās tu te || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.68"> jvaritānāṃ śunā sakhyaṃ kapisakhyaṃ tu śoṣiṇām |
                              <caesura/>
                               unmāde rākṣasaiḥ pretair apasmāre pravartanam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.69"> mehātisāriṇāṃ toyapānaṃ snehasya kuṣṭhinām |
                              <caesura/>
                               gulmeṣu sthāvarotpattiḥ koṣṭhe mūrdhni śiroruji || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.70"> śaṣkulībhakṣaṇaṃ chardyāmadhvā śvāsapipāsayoḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               haridraṃ bhojanaṃ vā'pi yasya syāt pāṇḍurogiṇaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.71"> raktapittī pibed yas tu śoṇitaṃ sa vinaśyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               svapnānevaṃvidhān dṛṣṭvā prātarutthāya yatnavān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.72"> dadyānmāṣāṃstilāṃllohaṃ viprebhyaḥ kāñcanaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               japec cāpi śubhān mantrān gāyatrīṃ tripadāṃ tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.73"> dṛṣṭvā tu prathame yāme svapyād dhyātvā punaḥ
                              śubham |
                              <caesura/>
                               japedvā'nyatamaṃ vede brahmacārī samāhitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.74"> devatāyatane caiva vasedrātritrayaṃ tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               viprāṃś ca pūjayennityaṃ duḥsvapnāt pravimucyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.75"> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi praśastaṃ svapnadarśanam |
                              <caesura/>
                               devān dvijān govṛṣabhān jīvataḥ suhṛdo nṛpān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.76"> samiddham agniṃ sādhūṃś ca nirmalāni jalāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               paśyet kalyāṇalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.77"> māṃsaṃ matsyān srajaḥ śvetā vāsāṃsi ca phalāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               labhante dhanalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.78"> mahāprāsādasaphalavṛkṣavāraṇaparvatān |
                              <caesura/>
                               āroheddravyalābhāya vyādherapagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79"> nadīnadasamudrāṃś ca kṣubhitān kaluṣodakān |
                              <caesura/>
                               taret kalyāṇalābhāya vyādher apagamāya ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79cdI"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.79cdII"/>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.80"> urago vā jalauko vā bhramaro vā'pi yaṃ daśet |
                              <caesura/>
                               ārogyaṃ nirdiśettasya dhanalābhaṃ ca buddhimān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.29.81"> evaṃrūpān śubhān svapnān yaḥ paśyed vyādhito naraḥ
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               sa dīrghāyur iti jñeyas tasmai karma samācaret || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              viparītāviparītasvapnanidarśanīyo nāmaikonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||
                         </p>
                    </div>




                    <div n="30" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.1"> athātaḥ pañcendriyārthavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ
                              vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.3"> śarīraśīlayor yasya prakṛter vikṛtir bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               tat tva riṣṭaṃ samāsena vyāsatas tu nibodha me || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.4"> śṛṇoti vividhān śabdān yo divyānām abhāvataḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               samudrapurameghānām asaṃpattau ca niḥsvanān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.5"> tān svanānnāvagṛhṇāti manyate cānyaśabdavat |
                              <caesura/>
                               grāmyāraṇyasvanāṃś cāpi viparītān śṛṇoti ca || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.6"> dviṣacchabdeṣu ramate suhṛcchabdeṣu kupyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               na śṛṇoti ca yo 'kasmāttaṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.7"> yas tūṣṇam iva gṛhṇāti śītamuṣṇaṃ ca śītavat |
                              <caesura/>
                               saṃjātaśītapiḍako yaś ca dāhena pīḍyate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.8"> uṣṇagātro 'timātraṃ ca yaḥ śītena pravepate |
                              <caesura/>
                               prahārān nābhijānāti yo 'ṅgacchedamathāpi vā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.9"> pāṃśunevāvakīrṇāni yaś ca gātrāṇi manyate |
                              <caesura/>
                               varṇānyatā vā rājyo vā yasya gātre bhavanti hi || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.10"> snātānuliptaṃ yaṃ cāpi bhajante nīlamakṣikāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               sugandhirvā'ti yo 'kasmāt taṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.11"> viparītena gṛhṇāti rasān yaś copayojitān |
                              <caesura/>
                               upayuktāḥ kramādyasya rasā doṣābhivṛddhaye || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.12"> yasya doṣāgnisāmyaṃ ca kuryur mithyopayojitāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               yo vā rasān na saṃvetti gatāsuṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.13"> sugandhaṃ vetti durgandhaṃ durgandhasya sugandhitām
                              |
                              <caesura/>
                               gṛhṇīte vā 'nyathā gandhaṃ śānte dīpe ca nīrujaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.14"> yo vā gandhān na jānāti gatāsuṃ taṃ vinirdiśet |
                              <caesura/>
                               dvandvānyuṣṇahimādīni kālāvasthā diśas tathā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.15"> viparītena gṛhṇāti bhāvān anyāṃś ca yo naraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               divā jyotīṃṣi yaś cāpi jvalitānīva paśyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.16"> rātrau sūryaṃ jvalantaṃ vā divā vā candravarcasam |
                              <caesura/>
                               ameghopaplave yaś ca śakracāpataḍidguṇān || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.17"> taḍittvato 'sitān yo vā nirmale gagane ghanān |
                              <caesura/>
                               vimānayānaprāsādair yaś ca saṃkulamambaram || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.18"> yaś cānilaṃ mūrtimantam antarikṣaṃ ca paśyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhūmanīhāravāsobhir āvṛtām iva medinīm || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.19"> pradīptam iva lokaṃ ca yo vā plutam ivāmbhasā |
                              <caesura/>
                               bhūmim aṣṭāpadākārāṃ lekhābhir yaś ca paśyati || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.20"> na paśyati sanakṣatrāṃ yaś cā devīm arundhatīm |
                              <caesura/>
                               dhruvam ākāśagaṅgāṃ vā taṃ vadanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.21"> jyotsnādarśoṣṇatoyeṣu chāyāṃ yaś ca na paśyati |
                              <caesura/>
                               paśyaty ekāṅgahīnāṃ vā vikṛtāṃ vā'nyasattvajām || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22"> śvakākakaṅkagṛdhrāṇāṃ pretānāṃ yakṣarakṣasām |
                              <caesura/>
                               piśācoraganāgānāṃ bhūtānāṃ vikṛtām api || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.30.23"> yo vā mayūrakaṇṭhābhaṃ vidhūmaṃ vahnim īkṣate |
                              <caesura/>
                               āturasya bhaven mṛtyuḥ svastho vyādhim āvāpnuyāt || </l>


                         <p xml:id="SS.1.30.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              pañcendriyārthavipratipattir nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                    </div>


                    <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
                         <head> ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.1"> athātaś chāyāvipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.3"> śyāvā lohitikā nīlā pītikā vā'pi mānavam |
                              <caesura/>
                               abhidravanti yaṃ chāyāḥ sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4"> hrīr apakramate yasya prabhādhṛtismṛtiśriyaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               akasmād yaṃ bhajante vā sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5"> yasyādharauṣṭhaḥ patitaḥ kṣiptaś cordhvaṃ
                              tathottaraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ubhau vā jāmbavābhāsau durlabhaṃ tasya jīvitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6"> āraktā daśanā yasya śyāvā vā syuḥ patanti vā |
                              <caesura/>
                               khañjanapratimā vā'pi taṃ gatāyuṣam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7"> kṛṣṇā stabdhā'valiptā vā jihvā śūnā ca yasya vai |
                              <caesura/>
                               karkaśā vā bhavedyasya so 'cirād vijahāty asūn || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8"> kuṭilā sphuṭitā vā'pi śuṣkā vā yasya nāsikā |
                              <caesura/>
                               avasphūrjati magnā vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9"> saṃkṣipte viṣame stabdhe rakte sraste ca locane |
                              <caesura/>
                               syātāṃ vā prasrute yasya sa gatāyurnaro dhruvam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.10"> keśāḥ sīmantino yasya saṃkṣipte vinate bhruvau |
                              <caesura/>
                               lunanti cākṣipakṣmāṇi so 'cirādyāti mṛtyave || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.11"> nāharaty annam āsyasthaṃ na dhārayati yaḥ śiraḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               ekāgradṛṣṭir mūḍhātmā sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.12"> balavān durbalo vā'pi saṃmohaṃ yo 'dhigacchati |
                              <caesura/>
                               utthāpyamāno bahuśastaṃ pakvaṃ bhiṣagādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13"> uttānaḥ sarvadā śete pādau vikurute ca yaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               viprasāraṇaśīlo vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.14"> śītapādakarocchvāsaś chinnocchvāsaś ca yo bhavet |
                              <caesura/>
                               kākocchvāsaś ca yo martyas taṃ dhīraḥ parivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.15"> nidrā na chidyate yasya yo vā jāgarti sarvadā |
                              <caesura/>
                               muhyed vā vaktukāmaś ca pratyākhyeyaḥ sa jānatā || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16"> uttarauṣṭhaṃ ca yo lihyād utkārāṃś ca karoti yaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               pretair vā bhāṣate sārdhaṃ pretarūpaṃ tam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17"> svebhyaḥ saromakūpebhyo yasya raktaṃ pravartate |
                              <caesura/>
                               puruṣasyāviṣārtasya sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18"> vātāṣṭhīlā tu hṛdaye yasyor dhvam anuyāyinī |
                              <caesura/>
                               rujā'nnavidveṣakarī sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19"> ananyopadravakṛtaḥ śophaḥ pādasamutthitaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               puruṣaṃ hanti nārīṃ tu mukhajo guhyajo dvayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20"> atisāro jvaro hikkā chardiḥ śūnāṇḍameḍhratā |
                              <caesura/>
                               śvāsinaḥ kāsino vā'pi yasya taṃ kṣīṇam ādiśet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21"> svedo dāhaś ca balavān hikkā śvāsaś ca mānavam |
                              <caesura/>
                               balavantam api prāṇair viyuñjanti na saṃśayaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22"> śyāvā jihvā bhaved yasya savyaṃ cākṣi nimajjati |
                              <caesura/>
                               mukhaṃ ca jāyate pūti yasya taṃ parivarjayet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23"> vaktram āpūryate 'śrubhiḥ svidyataś caraṇāv ubhau |
                              <caesura/>
                               cakṣuś cākulatāṃ yāti yamarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24"> atimātraṃ laghūni syur gātrāṇi gurukāṇi vā |
                              <caesura/>
                               yasyākasmāt sa vijñeyo gantā vaivasvatālayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25"> paṅkamatsyavasātailaghṛtagandhāṃś ca ye narāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               mṛṣṭagandhāṃś ca ye vānti gantāras te yamālayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26"> yūkā lalāṭam āyānti baliṃ nāśnanti vāyasāḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               yeṣāṃ vā'pi ratir nāsti yātāras te yamālayam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27"> jvarātisāraśophāḥ syur yasyānyonyāvasādinaḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya nāsau śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28"> kṣīṇasya yasya kṣuttṛṣṇe hṛdyair miṣṭair hitais
                              tathā |
                              <caesura/>
                               na śāmyato 'nnapānaiś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29"> pravāhikā śiraḥśūlaṃ koṣṭhaśūlaṃ ca dāruṇam |
                              <caesura/>
                               pipāsā balahāniś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30"> viṣameṇopacāreṇa karmabhiś ca purākṛtaiḥ |
                              <caesura/>
                               anityatvāc ca jantūnāṃ jīvitaṃ nidhanaṃ vrajet || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31"> pretā bhūtāḥ piśācāś ca rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca |
                              <caesura/>
                               maraṇābhimukhaṃ nityam upasarpanti mānavam || </l>

                         <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32"> tāni bheṣajavīryāṇi pratighnanti jighāṃsayā |
                              <caesura/>
                               tasmān moghāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā bhavanty eva gatāyuṣām || </l>
                         <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                              chāyāvipratipattirnāmaikatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
